Japan's Declaration of Treaty Abolition and the Future of East Asian Issues

— Wang Jiyuan

Since the Second Preparatory Conference for the London Naval Treaty began on October 23, it has presented a bleak and gloomy picture. Although triangular negotiations between the United States and Japan, Britain and the United States, and Britain and Japan have continued, the positions of the three countries and the points of contention at the conference have not changed in the slightest. Japan, with its offensive strategy, has loudly proclaimed the abolition of the principle of ratios and its replacement with the right to equal national defense. The United States, citing the length of its coastline and the need to maintain the Open Door Policy in East Asia, has firmly opposed changing the existing ratios. Britain, with its sophisticated tactics, has taken a mediatory position, engaging in shuttle diplomacy between the two sides. The conference has progressed from technical disputes to probes into the three parties' political opinions, and from the confrontation of political views back to the sticking points of technical issues, circulating back and forth for nearly two months. It was not until the news of the Japanese Privy Council's passage of the treaty abolition reached them that the negotiations were adjourned indefinitely on December 19.

Like a thunderbolt, Japan's formal notification of the abolition of the naval treaty was issued on December 29. The remnants of the Washington Naval Treaty have now been torn to shreds by Japan!

Japan's preparations for treaty abolition have been underway for some time. The reason for the delay in publishing it was, on the one hand, to use this as a surprise move, to make the British and American countries automatically concede on interests in the Far East, and automatically declare the modification of the Washington Naval Treaty; on the other hand, to unite with France and Italy to take a unified action of declaring abandonment, in order to strengthen momentum. Later, as a result of talks between Foreign Minister Hirota and the French and Italian ambassadors to Japan, both governments were unwilling to make such a statement. Japan was left with no choice but to make a unilateral declaration of abandoning the treaty at the end of last year, and revealed that it held two reasons: (1) It believed that when the Washington Treaty was signed, it was still impossible for the enemy's fleet to attack Japan by passing through the Pacific Ocean. Now, however, it is not the case. In recent years, the naval community has conducted repeated research and naval exercises, proving that the Pacific Ocean can not only be crossed, but also that in a Pacific naval battle, the fleet with a numerical advantage will certainly win; (2) It believed that since the establishment of "Manchukuo," the situation in East Asia has undergone a change, and the current world political situation is also very tense, which is enough to threaten Japan's position in East Asia. Therefore, the treaty is no longer in line with the needs of the times and will in the future cause defects in Japan's national defense. Therefore, it decided to abandon the treaty at the opportunity of its expiration in 1936. In fact, this kind of argument is enough to show its aggressive ambitions. Japan is really responsible for the tension in East Asian politics. This is self-evident without debate. Judging from the current Japanese naval power and the situation in various countries, it is even more evident that Britain and the United States have no possibility or need to attack Japan: In our opinion, although Japan is exercising its right to declare abandonment based on the treaty, its effect is nothing more than two points:

First, since the September 18th Incident, Japan has occupied our four northeastern provinces by force, established a puppet state, and at the same time, declared its withdrawal from the League of Nations, and further made a statement of monopolizing East Asia. The attitudes of various countries vary, and none dare to touch its reversed scales. Japan also knows that the whole world is swept into the tide of recession, and various countries must be unwilling to argue with it for too long at this time. Therefore, it is the time to declare the abolition of the treaty. After the Washington Naval Treaty is abandoned, Japan can not only freely manufacture warships according to its objective environmental needs, but also use its powerful naval power to expand its external aggression and blockade the Western Pacific, so that once a war breaks out, the warships of various countries, if they do not take risks, cannot cross the Lei Chi step.

Second, since the Washington Naval Treaty has been abandoned, the Four-Power Treaty, which was signed at the same time as the Washington Treaty, and the Four-Power Agreement, has in fact lost its effectiveness. The Open Door Policy must be re-examined, and new treaties must be redrafted to limit naval forces in the Pacific. Not only has the Washington Treaty system collapsed, but the League of Nations' control over the Pacific has also been destroyed in one fell swoop. The issue of Japan's return of the Pacific mandated territory in February and March of this year need not be discussed.

Therefore, although Japan's declaration of treaty abolition is only a legal action based on the treaty, its significance is extremely important. It cannot be discussed separately from the naval contraction negotiations, nor can it be separated from any issue in the Pacific. Its impact on the future of East Asian political issues is even greater. The center of the naval contraction issue from now on has progressed to how to clean up this fragmented situation and establish a flexible compromise in order to maintain temporary tranquility in the Pacific. As for the China issue, British Foreign Secretary Simon once said in his speech: "The British government believes that what is most important to world peace is that the naval powers with special interests and special responsibilities in the Far East continue to coordinate the limitation of naval forces and engage in cooperation with a collection system aimed at maintaining friendly relations between countries within the Far East." Simon's words have exposed the key issues in the naval conference. Since Japan has proudly declared the abolition of the treaty, the issue from now on is nothing more than how to carry out the method of jointly handling China.

Regarding the solution to East Asian issues, there have been two ambiguous trends in the preparatory meeting for the naval contraction. On the one hand, Japan has been trying its best to collude with Britain, using investment in Manchuria and guaranteeing interests in East Asia as bait, attempting to revive the dead ashes of the Anglo-Japanese alliance, in order to exclude the influence of third countries in China. The British Conservative Party, which is firmly embracing overseas market expansionism, is also happy to cooperate with it. On the other hand, the United States is calling for close cooperation between Britain and the United States by maintaining the Open Door Policy in the Far East, and advocating the expansion of the Pacific Three-Power Conference to establish a Pan-Pacific Coordination of Britain, the United States, Japan, France, Italy, and Russia, to incorporate the naval technical issues into the conditions for solving political issues. The Japanese mocked this attempt by the United States as "wishful thinking." In fact, the time when the objective conditions for Anglo-American cooperation are ripe is still far away. Moreover, in terms of the relationship between Britain and the United States, the Far East issue must not be compared with the "ship type" and "total tonnage" issues. In terms of the relationship between Britain and Japan, the Far East political issue and the technical issue must be integrated into one. In addition, the activities of France, Italy, Germany, and Russia in the Far East are also facts that cannot be ignored.

Therefore, the focus of the East Asian issue at present is: (1) Anglo-American cooperation? (2) Anglo-Japanese combination? (3) Or the universal coordination of countries with special interests and special responsibilities in the Far East? The collection system pointed out by Foreign Minister Simon clearly refers to the solution of the Far East issue must take the third path, at least the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan must establish a triangular relationship in a friendly manner. Only in this way can the stalemate of the naval contraction conference be broken, and the debate on military equality and the ratio principle, battleships and auxiliary ships, can establish a new agreement.

Now Japan has formally notified the abolition of the treaty! The representatives of the London Naval Contraction Preparatory Meeting will also quietly return to their home countries. The tragic first act of the naval contraction has been declared over. The issue from now on has shifted to the compromise of opinions on the East Asian issue. Our country, with no strong navy, has become the meat on the chopping board for the great powers to covet. Will our countrymen silently endure the slaughter of the great powers, or will they think about working hard, identify their goals, and prepare to resist foreign aggression! On the occasion of the New Year's renewal and the arrival of the 24th year of the Republic of China, I dare to ask this question to the people of the country.

A Review of World Politics in 1934

— Ren Xiang

It has been six years since the postwar world fell into the abyss of total panic. In this year of 1935, we look back at the world politics of the past year. Compared with the beginning of the panic, what kind of changes have taken place in its content? Generally speaking, world politics is moving towards an increasingly acute stage year by year. That trend is very clear. Let's not talk about the years before 1930. Starting from 1931, the main political struggles in Europe were hidden behind the financial turmoil, drawing Vienna, Berlin, and London into the center of the vortex. In 1932, the German Nazi Party movement gradually rose, and the call for military equality was also put forward at that time. This of course reflected that the competition for hegemony in Central Europe had entered a new stage. At the beginning of 1933, the first thing that happened was that Hitler seized power in Germany. As a result, European politics changed direction. Later, the attempt by the great powers to compromise proved to be a complete failure at the London Economic Conference in July. And the outcome of Britain's mediation of German and French armaments only resulted in France's rapprochement with the Soviet Union. Germany's withdrawal from disarmament and the League of Nations were all inevitable. At this time, Austria and Italy joined together, which proved that new storms were brewing in Central Europe and Southeastern Europe. Now we look back at the European political situation in 1934. The content of its disputes has of course been further advanced. Secondly, in the Pacific, we can see the same overall situation. After the September 18th Incident (1931), followed by the outbreak of the January 28th Sino-Japanese War in Shanghai, the contradictory relations between the great powers in the Pacific became tense step by step. By February 1933, Japan had advanced into Jehol, and the Tanggu Truce was concluded. On the one hand, Japan had announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations. On the other hand, the League of Nations' technical cooperation plan in China was being launched. In the same year, several things happened that were related to the overall situation in the Pacific. The first was the establishment of the London Silver Agreement in July. The second was the restoration of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia in November. We compare these experiences with the Far Eastern politics of 1934. Of course, we can see that the contradictory relations between the great powers in the Pacific are still developing.

What are the fundamental reasons for the tension between the great powers today? Generally speaking, there are about two points. First, the great powers have strengthened their seizure of colonial interests. Because the main goal of world politics under the control of the great powers today is the control of capital and commodity markets. Therefore, conflicts caused by the seizure of colonies are inevitable. Second, the domestic economies of the great powers are unstable. At present, major countries such as Britain, the United States, Germany, France, Japan, and Italy have all suffered heavy blows in terms of production. Therefore, a large number of unemployed people have emerged. Domestic economic instability is a major cause of the antagonistic state of international relations. These are the two essential perspectives we use to explain world politics in 1934.

Now we have to give a rough outline of the important contents of the world political situation in 1934.

In the Pacific, the first thing that deserves our attention is the naval conference of the British Empire in Singapore (January 26). The convening of this conference pointed out that Britain and Japan are competing in the Indian Ocean and Pacific markets. The construction of Britain's eastern Gibraltar and Japan's military deployments are reflecting each other in succession. Japan's attempt to dig through the Kra Isthmus in Siam not only caused panic in Singapore, but also caused anxiety in Siam. Secondly, since 1933, the great powers have been reluctant to give up their influence because they are afraid of the expansion of Japanese power. Therefore, Japan issued the Amau Doctrine on April 17, 1934. On the one hand, this has had some impact on the League of Nations' technical cooperation plan. On the other hand, it is forcing China to yield. Under this situation, Japan's military equipment is becoming more and more obvious not only in Northeast China and Inner Mongolia, but also in other places. Again, how Japan's leading power in East Asia is naturally closely related to her naval military equipment. Therefore, the naval contraction preparatory conference convened in London in October 1934 had to make the confrontation between Japan and the United States an undeniable fact due to Japan's strong demands. The Washington Treaty was therefore abolished. This is tantamount to saying publicly that the foundation of peace in the Pacific has been completely sacrificed under the power of military competition.

In 1934, the state of entanglement in European politics seemed to be even more tense than in the Pacific. The first shocking thing in this year was the suppression of the Austrian Nazi Party by Dollfuss in January. The reason why Austria did this was of course due to "having nothing to fear" internationally. However, Germany could not be reconciled to this. Therefore, in the coup on July 25, Dollfuss was sacrificed in this dispute. Fortunately, the Nazi Party was quick-witted and changed course, and the evil storm in Vienna dissipated immediately. However, there is still one point worth noting. That is, the joint action against Austria that Britain, France, and Italy have been advocating for years has obviously reduced its color compared to before 1934. This mainly illustrates the expansion of the rivalry between France and Italy in Central and Southeastern Europe.

Everyone knows that French Foreign Minister Barthou's policy was to consolidate the Versailles system. Therefore, on the one hand, he made friends with the Soviet Union and advocated the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. On the other hand, he united the Balkan and Central European Little Entente countries to achieve the effect of 指臂. However, Poland therefore approached Germany, and the situation in Southeastern Europe became even more tense. In October, King Alexander of Yugoslavia and French Foreign Minister Barthou had to be sacrificed by their enemies in Marseille. This was another tragic scene.

Amidst such turmoil in Europe, the relationship between France and the Soviet Union has developed further. This is the event of the Soviet Union joining the League of Nations on September 18, 1934. The Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations was brewing at a time when Britain was mediating between German and French armaments in order to suppress Germany. That is a fact that everyone knows. The realization of this event clearly indicates whether the breakdown of European peace is imminent. However, in this situation, Germany has even more difficulties in maintaining peace. If her domestic political disputes are not as moderate as they are now, I am afraid that the peace of the overall European situation will not be maintained to this day.

From the Pacific to Europe, we have given a rough outline of world politics in 1934 in the above. Looking forward to the world politics of the coming year, what will be the overall situation? Judging from the development of history, the current world has obviously entered a period of brewing that is epoch-making. The arms race in the Pacific is a very important feature of 1935. Secondly, the internal political changes and diplomatic tensions in European countries will probably advance simultaneously with 1935. If we combine these two aspects, it cannot be regarded as a general threat to world peace for mankind. As for how to realize the plan for maintaining world peace, I think it is always a common responsibility for the people of the world in 1935.

Implementation Plan for National Products Education

— Pan Wenan

In recent years, China has suffered deeply from the economic aggression of various countries, leading the national economy into a desperate situation. To seek fundamental relief, the people of the country have called for resisting foreign goods and promoting domestic products. However, resisting foreign goods is a passive preventive method, while promoting domestic products is the ultimate active remedy. Simply advocating resistance without real strength is futile; active promotion embodies the profound intention of revitalizing industry and resisting foreign goods.

This year, enthusiastic individuals in Shanghai, in conjunction with the national products and education sectors, have further designated this year as "Student National Products Year" to increase the effectiveness of promoting domestic products. This intention is excellent. Therefore, a "National Products Education Implementation Plan" is proposed as a reference for schools in various regions, outlined as follows:

A. Administrative Aspects:

1. Regarding Schools:

(1) Schools should, as a primary principle, adopt domestic products for educational stationery, student uniforms, and all other necessary supplies.

(2) Promulgate measures to reward students for purchasing domestic goods and prohibit students from purchasing foreign goods. (Each school can freely determine these.)

(3) Establish a National Products Salvation Administrative Committee: such as National Products Consumption Week, National Products Exhibition Week, National Products Investigation Week, National Products Factory Visit Week, National Products Lecture Week, etc., so that the entire school has a central task of promoting domestic products and saving the country every week or month.

(4) Arrange a school environment that promotes domestic products and saves the country: various surveys and statistics on domestic product industries, statistics on the economic losses suffered by China from various countries, and other charts, murals, photographs, slogans, etc., related to the promotion of domestic products and saving the country; to startle young people and inspire them to strive.

(5) Stipulate research work and equipment, such as research on the development of Chinese national product industries, the relationship between promoting national products and the national economy, an overview of foreign goods sales in China and the losses suffered by China, the situation of foreign goods imports and domestic goods exports, the methods and steps for promoting domestic products, research on various domestic product raw materials; and the equipment of national product exhibition rooms and factories, etc.

(6) Use memorial weeks and commemorative days to read vows of love for domestic products, hold national product lectures, sing songs promoting domestic products, shout slogans promoting domestic products, etc., to stimulate students' determination to promote domestic products and save the country.

(7) Use memorial holidays to reward students and send them to various places to publicize, thereby awakening public understanding and attention.

(8) Establish a special National Products Salvation Lecture Series, inviting famous people to talk about the development of various Chinese national product industries and the paths for the development of various Chinese national product industries, etc., to awaken students' recognition and attention.

(9) Schools should earnestly contact domestic product manufacturers, such as national product introductions, sample displays, factory visits, etc., to increase the effectiveness of promoting national products and saving the country.

(10) Publish various publications related to national products and saving the country; such as a list of national product manufacturers, a list of domestic products,

Page 12

periodicals introducing national products, etc., to instill in students all kinds of knowledge about national products.

2. Regarding Faculty and Staff:

(1) All faculty and staff should uniformly strive to carry out the school's established policies and enthusiastically participate in all school national product activities.

(2) All faculty and staff should uniformly lead by example, wear domestic product uniforms, and publicize national product salvation, making themselves models for all students.

(3) Should live with the students, regardless of diet and daily life, to facilitate the effectiveness of national product guidance.

(4) Guide students in all activities promoting national products.

(5) Should use holidays to visit and investigate domestic product factories and businesses to increase service effectiveness.

(6) Should seek earnest contact with domestic product manufacturers.

B. Teaching Aspects:

1. Regarding Teaching Materials:

(1) Select and read the words, deeds, biographies, and success stories of pioneers in the national products sector and inventors of new industrial products.

(2) Select and read articles and poems promoting domestic products.

(3) Create more articles on national products salvation.

(4) Study the manufacturing methods of everyday national product goods and the sources of their raw materials, etc.

(5) Study the manufacturing methods of industrial products that substitute for foreign goods and the sources of their raw materials, etc.

(6) Emphasize the physical and chemical knowledge applied when manufacturing national product goods.

(7) Collect historical materials on the economic oppression suffered by our country from various countries throughout history.

(8) Pay attention to research on the development of national product industries.

(9) Investigate the status of national product promotion in various regions.

(10) Study the relationship between promoting national products and transportation.

(11) Study the products and raw materials of various regions in our country.

(12) Study the economic policies and industrial conditions of various countries.

(13) Create charts and statistics on various national product industries.

(14) Calculate the quantity of auxiliary materials for various national product manufactured goods.

(15) Draw pictures, advertisements, and publicity paintings promoting national product salvation.

(16) Draw maps of the sources of supply for various domestic raw materials.

(17) Select and learn songs of national product salvation.

2. Regarding Extracurricular Activities:

(1) Hold visits and investigations: such as national product factories, national product companies, etc., to enhance students' research interest, practical experience, and understanding of national products.

(2) Organize domestic product consumption associations, national product improvement associations, national product raw material research associations, etc., to enhance students' understanding and efforts towards national products.

(3) Hold thematic research: such as how to develop national product industries, how to promote national products, the relationship between promoting national products and transportation, etc., to develop students' creative abilities.

(4) Hold national product investigations: what kinds of goods are national products, what kinds of goods are foreign goods, and further research industries that substitute for foreign goods.

(5) Use holidays to go to various places to give speeches on the importance of national product salvation and promotional activities such as masquerade performances. To awaken the public's awareness.

(6) Practice the manufacturing methods of everyday national product goods, etc.

Reorganization of Jiangsu Finance

— Zhao Dihua

I. Introduction

Jiangsu has long been known as a region of wealth, with abundant products and developed commerce. However, in recent years, the situation has changed. Not only is the private economy in a state of distress, but the public finances are also like a family in decline. Although the facade remains, the actual strength is exhausted, stretched to the limit, and resources are depleted. As for the development of enterprises, it is even more out of the question. The author, a native of Jiangsu, deeply doubts why the financial strength of Jiangsu Province has declined to this extent, and has tried to investigate the reasons without success. Last winter, I was ordered to manage the finances of Jiangsu Province, and I am not without trepidation in shouldering this important task. However, the doubts of the past can be verified with actual practice, and a reorganization plan can be established based on this, proceeding step by step. The extent to which it can accomplish its tasks is unpredictable, but day by day, month by month, it will naturally be able to promote benefits to the fullest. This is discussed in four sections, so that a glimpse of the reorganization of Jiangsu Province's finances over the past year can be seen.

II. Principles for Reorganizing Finances

Reorganizing finances cannot be achieved overnight. Proceeding step by step, its effects will be seen naturally. The principles of reorganization are divided into provincial and county levels:

1. Provincial Finance

A. Unified Revenue and Expenditure: In the past, the actual situation of provincial finance was that in terms of revenue and expenditure management, each agency handled its own affairs in the name of special funds, each using its source of income to allocate its use. Those with more income would expand their expenditure as much as possible, and the waste of public funds was considerable. Those with less income were deeply afraid of insufficient revenue and strived to open up sources of income, thereby increasing the burden on the people. Both have their drawbacks. If revenue and expenditure can be unified, the province's finances will have a complete system, adjusting surpluses and deficits, planning comprehensively, impartially, and allowing various enterprises to develop evenly and progress step by step. In order to implement unified revenue and expenditure, the "Measures for the Custody and Disbursement of Special Provincial Funds" were formulated to achieve unification.

B. Establish a Budget: The budget is the compass of financial administration. In terms of general effectiveness, (1) it can determine the standard for the government's future operations, (2) it is a tool for rectifying income and restricting excessive expenditure, (3) it is evidence of credibility with the people, and (4) it expresses the government's administrative plan, making various enterprises easier to manage. Since the effectiveness of the budget is as described above, it should be based on facts when preparing it. If it involves any superficiality, it will become a tool for deceiving the world. Jiangsu Province's provincial budget includes all revenue and expenditure. The income side can be divided into three major categories:

(1) Ordinary Provincial Taxes: These are the land tax, business tax, and deed tax, now plus the tobacco and alcohol license tax.

(2) Various Special Funds: There are two types: education and construction. Education is funded by the land tax, slaughter tax, and brokerage tax. Construction is funded by the land tax and business income, etc.

(3) Other Income: This includes central government subsidies, income from Sha Tian official property, and judicial or miscellaneous income.

Expenditure includes: Party affairs, administration, judiciary, public security, finance, education, industry, construction, health assistance fees, etc. In the past, the provincial budget failed to include all revenue and expenditure, so the entire situation could not be expressed. Starting from the 22nd year, all revenue and expenditure will be compiled to achieve unification.

C. Strictly Implement the Treasury System: In the past, Jiangsu Province's treasury was represented by four banks: Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Jiangsu Bank, and Farmers Bank. According to regulations, all provincial funds received should be deposited into the treasury immediately, but this could not be done in practice. Sometimes it was delayed for several months before being deposited after repeated reminders. During the delay, the county magistrate could deposit it into a private account to generate interest, so the establishment of the treasury failed to achieve its effect. Since the establishment of county accounting directors in the 22nd year, they have been responsible for supervising the deposit of funds into the treasury, and measures for the deposit of funds have been established with strict supervision. After several months of implementation, its effectiveness has become apparent.

D. Implement an Audit System: Pre-audit and post-audit are both important aspects of supervising finance. Jiangsu Province once established an audit committee, but it was soon abolished, resulting in unlimited expenditure by various agencies, which is not a prudent way to manage finances. Therefore, in March of the 22nd year, the "Organizational Regulations of the Audit Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Government" and "Audit Rules" were formulated. It is stipulated that: 1. The payment orders for the use of provincial and local funds should be signed by the committee. 2. The revenue and expenditure calculations of the provincial government and its directly affiliated agencies shall be audited by the committee. Although it has only been implemented for a short time in the 23rd year, it has indeed achieved the practical effect of supervising finance.

E. Reform the Land Tax System: The land tax system in Jiangsu Province has been deeply ingrained for a long time. It relies solely on clerks who secretly hold their private registers as a secret. The addresses of false households are unknown, and the mu (unit of area) are not accurate, allowing the clerks to arbitrarily add or hide land, resulting in land without tax, tax without land, or more land with less tax, and less land with more tax. All kinds of irregularities arise from this. Since last winter, preparations for reform have been underway. The following aspects are being carried out this year:

(1) Conduct Land Declaration: In November of last year, the department sent personnel to various counties to investigate and conduct on-site inspections, and it was decided to start with Zhenjiang, Yixing, Liyang, and Jiangyin counties first. After sufficient preparation and widespread publicity, it was started this spring, and the results are satisfactory. All household registers and plot registers have been compiled. In the 23rd year, they will be used as the basis for creating strings of tax tickets. Counties that continue to conduct land declarations include: Jurong, Taicang, Wujiang, Jintan, Jiangdu, Yancheng, Tongshan, Suining, Muyang, Pei County, Yangzhou Chongming, Xinghua, and Xiao County, are currently underway.

(2) Reorganize Land Tax Surcharges: Land tax surcharges in Jiangsu Province are extremely complex, as everyone knows. Statistics show that there are as many as 105 different types of surcharges in the province, and the surcharges exceed the regular tax by several times to ten times or more. Although some of this is due to the regular tax being too low, resulting in the surcharges being particularly heavy, its complexity and disorder are undeniable. It has been strictly reorganized in accordance with central government laws and regulations. In counties where land declarations are being conducted, the newly added land and its newly added surcharges are entirely used to offset the reduction of surcharges, as exemplified by Yixing, as shown in the table below.

(3) Change Collection Methods: The following points concern changes in the procedures for collecting land tax:

(1) Banks Collect Taxes on Behalf of the Government: The land tax in Jiangsu Province has been deeply mired in malpractices. Unscrupulous clerks take advantage of this to collect excessive taxes and embezzle the difference, which has become an open secret. Therefore, in the 23rd year, measures were established for banks to collect taxes on behalf of the government, so that taxes are directly paid by taxpayers to the bank without going through the hands of clerks, thereby eliminating the malpractice of collecting excessive taxes and embezzlement. However, this measure is a newly established system, and for the sake of prudence, Zhenjiang, Wuxian, Yixing, Wujiang, Kunshan, Jiangyin, Shishan, and Jiading counties were designated to pilot the system first. In the months since then, the implementation has been relatively smooth.

(2) Change Tax Tickets from Silver to Yuan: In the past, the land tax in Jiangsu Province was calculated in silver, and the people paid their taxes in silver yuan. Taxpayers were unaware of how to calculate the exchange between silver and silver yuan, and clerks took advantage of this to collect excessive taxes. In order to eliminate this long-standing malpractice, strict orders have been issued to all counties to clearly state the mu (unit of area), tax rate, and amount of silver yuan payable on the tax tickets. People pay taxes according to the tax tickets, thereby reducing the malpractice of collecting excessive taxes.

(3) Pay Taxes at Counters: In order to facilitate tax payment for the people, branch counters have been established in the four rural areas in addition to the county's main counter. This allows taxpayers to pay their taxes at the counter nearby without having to go through clerks, which is a way to eliminate collecting excessive taxes and embezzlement.

2. County Finance

A. Reorganize the Budget: In the past, the budgets of various counties in Jiangsu Province were sent to the Department of Finance for review, but in reality, they were not reviewed, so the result was either fictitious revenue and actual expenditure, or falsely listed revenue and expenditure, which could not restrict calculations. The local agencies of various counties spent extravagantly, which was endless. In order to reorganize finances, the reorganization of the budget was first established as a principle.

B. Establish a Treasury: In the past, the cash revenue and expenditure procedures were extremely chaotic. The powers of tax collection agencies, management agencies, and expenditure agencies were not clearly defined. Since July of this year, county treasuries have been established. All revenue and expenditure of county local funds are managed by the treasury. Measures for the revenue, expenditure, and storage of county funds and the "Provisional Regulations for County Treasuries in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province" have been established to delineate them. In this way, the malpractice of mutual transfer of provincial and county funds in the past is completely eliminated.

C. Revise the Accounting System: Each county establishes an accounting director to manage accounting. All county government expenditures, fund reports, fund offsets, and loans, receipts, and contracts must be signed, countersigned, and stamped, and the county magistrate is jointly responsible. The accounting he handles is divided into two parts: provincial funds and county funds.

D. Implement an Audit System: Detailed regulations have been formulated regarding budget execution and cash procedures. The audit agency may refuse to sign for payments exceeding the budget. Pre-audit is already thorough. Regulations have also been formulated for the preparation of revenue and expenditure calculation documents. Extravagant and illegal expenditures are eliminated, so that post-audit can also be executed based on them.

Based on the above principles, laws and regulations have been formulated, talents have been selected, and efforts have been made to implement them in the shortest possible time. The progress of the implementation is described in the next section. III. Progress of the Reorganization Work

The malpractices of Jiangsu Province's finances have been long-standing, so although the principles of improvement have been established, there are still many obstacles during the implementation. There are those who harbor doubts and those who obstruct. The province earnestly persuades and informs the general public to understand the meaning and benefits of reform. The major aspects of the reorganization work are as follows:

(1) Reform of the Budget: The reform of the provincial budget can be divided into the following four points:

A. Preparation Time: In the past, the provincial budget took a long time due to consultations between various responsible agencies, and by the time it was finally completed, the year was about to end, often losing its effectiveness. This time, the provincial budget was prepared to avoid this drawback.

B. Revenue Section: The 22nd year budget does not engage in fictitious assumptions, but relies entirely on reality. Therefore, the estimated revenue and the results are not too far apart.

C. Expenditure Section: Fixed items, such as the operating expenses of various agencies. Unfixed items, such as business expenses and temporary expenses. Before the general budget is established, each agency prepares a separate budget. After the separate budgets are reviewed and confirmed, the provincial budget is then compiled. This ensures that the foundation is correct and that there are no obstacles in executing the budget. This is also a reform of the budget preparation process.

The reform of the county budget can be divided into the following four points:

A. Review Procedures: Starting in November of the 22nd year, the Department of Finance organized county budget review committees to convene county magistrates from various counties to hold meetings for preliminary review, and the department also dispatched representatives to attend. After the preliminary review, each county immediately re-prepared a new budget based on the results of the review and submitted it to the provincial government meeting on schedule for final decision.

B. Estimate Revenue: Accurately calculate the land tax and other revenues to obtain a total revenue, and then calculate the total expenditure in order to form a balanced revenue and expenditure budget.

C. Reduce Expenditure: The general estimates listed by various counties all have extravagant and uneconomical expenditures, which have been greatly reduced. The principles for reduction are as follows:

(1) Agencies that are not necessary should be eliminated to save overall expenses.

(2) Expenditures that are uneconomical or not urgently needed should be deleted.

(3) Temporary expenditures should not be included in recurring expenses.

D. Determine Subjects: The names of land tax surcharges in various counties are numerous and should be unified urgently. Therefore, the budget reform is to summarize them into land tax county tax, and the distribution is indicated separately by a percentage ratio.

(2) Unified Accounting System: Each county establishes an accounting director to specifically handle tax accounting. All taxes collected by the county government must be entered into the accounts. Its characteristics are as follows:

A. This account book only records the receipt and deposit of taxes and does not involve expenditures.

B. This system becomes the center of county government accounting.

C. The function of the accounting statements focuses on the deposit and storage of cash.

D. The account book focuses on statistics, which are used to assess the performance of collection.

(3) Establish County Treasuries: All counties that have established branches or offices of the Farmers Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are entrusted as treasury agents. To date, 45 counties have been established, and they will need to be universally established in the future.

(4) Implement the Audit System: Pre-audit can be divided into budget audit and the issuance of payment orders. Post-audit involves the preparation of proof settlement documents and the audit of the final accounts. The audit of provincial and county funds is currently handled by two agencies:

Provincial - Implemented by the Audit Committee of the Provincial Government

County - Audited by the Department of Finance.

IV. Comparison of Past and Present Finances

Due to the failure to unify revenue and expenditure in the past financial situation of Jiangsu Province, the Department of Finance only managed a part of the finances, which made it impossible to collect complete statistics. Now, based on the revenue situation of provincial tax and land tax, comparing the past year with the 22nd year after reorganization, its revenue is as follows:

Actual revenue in the 21st year was about 9.85 million yuan.

Actual revenue in the 22nd year was about 11.97 million yuan

In addition to land tax, the largest revenue item is business tax. The business tax revenue in the 21st year was about 1.34 million yuan. The business tax revenue in the 22nd year was about 2.39 million yuan.

Judging from the past situation, the chaos in finance was not only due to the shortfalls in revenue, but the inability to establish a budget made the expectations for expenditure often far from reality. This illness caused the suspension of enterprises and the reduction of administrative efficiency. For example, the estimated revenue in the 21st year was 27 million yuan, while the actual revenue was only 18.75 million yuan. The budgeted revenue in the 22nd year was over 22 million yuan, and the actual revenue reached over 23 million yuan. (Including loans, about 28 million yuan.)

The revenue and expenditure situation of the province has been described above, and the revenue and expenditure situation of the county finances in various counties is difficult to obtain accurately and completely due to the lack of a unified accounting system in the past. In general, they are all cases of fictitious revenue and actual expenditure, and the accumulated losses over the years are considerable. The most contradictory aspect is that on the one hand, there is insufficient revenue for local enterprises, and on the other hand, the rural areas are desolate and urgently need to reduce the burden on the people. In fact, the difference between revenue and expenditure is far too great.

In terms of the past county financial administration, Jiangsu Province has undergone two changes. Its organization is

1. The county government is the main tax collection agency—the county government collects land tax deed tax (part of which is deposited into the province, and part of which is used for the county) and miscellaneous donations, and the education bureau and construction bureau collect part of the miscellaneous donations. The business tax, which was established not long ago, is collected by the Department of Finance.

2. The finance bureau is the main tax collection agency—the special point is that the finance bureau replaces the county government in collecting taxes (part of which is deposited into the province, and part of which is used for the county).

Both of the above systems have their drawbacks. Both are merely transfers of the power to collect taxes. The county magistrate can engage in corruption, and why would the bureau chief be any different? The shortcoming is the lack of supervisory agencies and checks and balances. Therefore, the Jiangsu Province finance is still in a state of chaos.

The author believes that in order for finance to move towards the right track, strict supervision should be implemented first to ensure that the chief accountant stands in a detached position. An accounting director is established outside the county government. At the same time, due to the establishment of the budget calculation system and the improvement of revenue and expenditure procedures, the duties of the accounting director are easier to perform, and the effect of the accounting system is apparent.

As a result of the reorganization, extravagant expenditures have been greatly reduced. On the revenue side, exorbitant and bothersome miscellaneous taxes and land tax surcharges have been abolished and reduced separately. The situation is shown in the following table

Abolish Exorbitant Taxes

In terms of the budget after the reorganization, the revenue and expenditure items of the counties are also unified. The total expenditure of the counties in the province in the 22nd year is estimated as follows:

1. Party affairs expenses are about 800,000 yuan

2. Civil affairs expenses are about 1.95 million yuan

3. Public security expenses are about 6.05 million yuan

4. Education and culture expenses are about 9.36 million yuan

There were no figures available for county local finance in the past. Since this reorganization, it is firmly believed that there is a path to follow. The above is a summary of the major steps in the reorganization of finance. Other efforts, such as unifying the collection of local donations, are also being made without reservation.

V. Expectations for the Future

For local finance to move towards the right track, it is not enough for those in charge of finance to implement measures to achieve great results. It is necessary for the people of the province to cooperate fully to achieve success. At the beginning of my tenure, I set the goal of financial transparency, so that everyone can trust the government. Only when they can trust the government can they implement government laws and regulations. Now that we have this foundation, we hope that all parties will work together. This is the first expectation.

The financial resources of the local area depend entirely on social order and market finance. If the people's livelihood cannot be stabilized and finance cannot be circulated, then the financial resources will definitely be in a state of distress. Conversely, the financial resources will definitely be abundant. The causal relationship between them is very obvious. The current policy guidelines of the provincial government are based on construction to promote the prosperity of social production, and on the other hand, to circulate finance and inject it into the rural areas. To promote the vitality of the collapsing social foundation, social order will gradually stabilize in the future, financial resources will be smooth, and all matters can be handled. This is the second expectation.

As for the various financial measures, those in charge are exhausting their intelligence to achieve considerable results. However, I am afraid that with a thousand considerations, there will still be one mistake. I hope that all clear-minded people in the country will always provide guidance to strive for perfection. This is even more deeply felt among all kinds of expectations.

Current Commentary

The Essentials of Promoting Domestically Produced Silk and Satin

— Ji

Over the past four or five years, the national crisis has grown increasingly urgent. It's not just that foreign aggression is severe and natural disasters are frequent, but the entire national economy has also fallen into a state of collapse and bankruptcy. As we approach the end of the year and welcome the new, shouldn't we, as Chinese people, seize this opportunity to rouse ourselves and strive for recovery? There is more than one way to rouse ourselves, but promoting domestic goods and reducing import surpluses is the most pressing task.

The Silk Industry Association and the Husha Art Society of this city, deeply aware of this, recently petitioned the central government to issue a nationwide decree that whenever commemorative weeks, important meetings, or joyous and sorrowful events are held, the dress code promulgated by the National Government on April 16, 1929, should be followed, and domestically produced silk ceremonial attire should be used. Today, on New Year's Day, Husha is also holding a ceremonial attire movement to showcase the elegance of domestically produced silk ceremonial attire. Clothing, food, shelter, and transportation are fundamental activities of people's lives, and proper attire can especially demonstrate the demeanor of a great nation. Chairman Chiang has taken it upon himself to promote the New Life Movement, saying, "Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame must be manifested in daily life." Unfortunately, among the Chinese people, regardless of age or gender, those who are ignorant of this principle are everywhere. Therefore, on holidays and festivals, when participating in grand ceremonies, some wear inappropriate attire, and some wear imported materials. Some even flaunt their attire in the streets, appearing pleased with themselves and losing all sense of national decorum. What a loss to national dignity! What an impact on the sales of domestic goods! In short, if this trend is not changed, it will not only be a disgrace to oneself but also harm people's livelihoods. Therefore, the promotion of this domestic silk ceremonial attire movement is highly commendable.

Chinese silk is inherently a noble material. Since the opening of trade with foreign countries, a great deal has been exported. However, in recent years, the techniques of sericulture, silkworm rearing, silk reeling, and silk weaving in our country have remained stagnant, with little improvement. Furthermore, with the prevalence of rayon and the competition from foreign silk fabrics, the overseas market has plummeted. As for the fashionable women in our country, they admire foreign goods and disdain domestically produced silk and satin. As a result, silk merchants are losing money, and silk factories are closing down everywhere. And how can we not worry about the millions of silkworm farmers who have gone bankrupt and workers who have lost their jobs? Thinking of this, I truly feel disheartened. The way to remedy this situation must depend on the awakening of the Chinese people. We must not abandon the sales of domestic silk because we love to wear Western suits. At this time of serious national crisis, even if we cannot endure hardship and prepare for battle, we should still promote patriotism and consider the national economy. Therefore, within our means, wearing domestically produced silk is our duty.

We also believe that promoting domestic silk need not be mutually exclusive with wearing Western suits. Those who love to wear Western suits generally do so because they are lightweight and attractive, not necessarily with the intention of abandoning their own culture and following others. Moreover, their choice of imported materials does not necessarily mean that they absolutely reject domestic products. Therefore, in order to break with convention, someone should try using domestically produced silk and satin to make Western clothing. At the same time, silk manufacturers should also strive to improve their products, so that their colors and textures are suitable for making Western clothing. In this way, the sales of domestic silk can be increased considerably. Otherwise, even if we absolutely prohibit Chinese people from wearing Western suits, the sales of domestically produced silk will still inevitably be encroached upon by foreign goods.

Qu Fangpu Visits Chiang, Reports on Situation in Southwest, Negotiations on Guangdong Affairs Proceed Smoothly, Qu Already Left Hangzhou for Shanghai Yesterday

Chiang Receives Huang Shaoxiong, Inquires About Governance Policies

Hangzhou: Qu Fangpu, Director of the Guangdong Department of Finance, accompanied by Yang Dezhao, arrived in Hangzhou the day before yesterday and stayed at the Xileng Hotel. This morning, he visited Chairman Chiang to report on the situation in the Southwest and conduct negotiations on Guangdong affairs. The results were very satisfactory. Qu and Yang took the express train to Shanghai at 2:00 PM today. Qu will then transfer from Shanghai to Guangdong. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Hangzhou: This morning, Chiang received Xu Shaodi, Xu Qingfu, Zhou Xiangxian, Zhao Longwen, and others, inquiring in detail about education and finance in Zhejiang, as well as municipal administration and public security in Hangzhou. At 9:00 PM, he also summoned Huang Shaoxiong to inquire about the policies for new government facilities for about an hour. It was decided that he would attend the swearing-in ceremony of all members of the provincial government at 10:00 AM tomorrow morning and give a speech. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Hangzhou: Yang Yongtai, Ye Chucang, and Zhang Jingjiang left for Shanghai by early train today. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Hong Kong: Qu Fangpu telegraphed that he left Hangzhou for Shanghai on the afternoon of the 31st and will return to Guangdong by ship on the morning of the 1st. If he can't make it, he will depart on the 5th. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Hong Kong: Li Zongren will come to Hong Kong to meet Hu Hanmin. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Local Authorities Hold New Year's Day Group Greetings

Tianjin Implements New Year's Security Measures

Tianjin: The Tianjin Public Security Bureau will implement New Year's security measures for five days starting today. All police teams in each district will be fully mobilized for security. The Hebei Provincial Government will hold group greetings for the provincial government and all department staff at the auditorium at 9:00 AM on New Year's Day. There will be a three-day holiday, and office work will be suspended. However, the reception of foreign guests will be declined. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

Reports from the Central Government and National Government Memorial Weeks

Yang Jie: Reflections After Inspecting Military Preparations

Lin Sen: Political Work Over the Past Year

Nanjing: The Central Government held its 163rd Memorial Week at 9:00 AM on the 31st. Ju Zheng, Yang Jie, Hong Ludaong, Li Ciwen, Zhu Jiqing, Fang Juehui, Li Zonghuang, and all staff members, totaling about 500 people, attended. Ju Zheng presided. Yang Jie reported "Reflections After Inspecting Military Preparations in Various Countries," stating that all European and American countries are striving to improve their military preparations and strengthen their national defenses. To establish a nation in modern times, it is not enough to be rich and strong; without military power, it is impossible to resist foreign aggression. However, to become rich and strong, we must first implement an industrial revolution and concentrate national power. Only then can military preparations be sufficient. If military power is insufficient, we must use diplomacy as a barrier. Strong diplomatic functions can serve as a route of aggression, while weak ones can serve as protection for the country. To achieve these two goals, appropriate intelligence and material resources are prerequisites. The world crisis is imminent. Modern warfare has been transformed into three-dimensional warfare due to the development of the air force. If war occurs, the entire country will be a battlefield, with no distinction between front and rear. Politicians in various countries are now using diplomacy to avoid war. At this juncture, our country must emulate the efforts of European and American countries to prepare military power and strengthen national defense in order to survive in today's world and overcome the current world crisis. The meeting adjourned at 10:00 AM. (Central News Agency Dispatch from the 31st)

Nanjing: The National Government held Memorial Week at 31:00 AM. He Yingqin, Zhang Ji, Chen Qicai, Wang Yongbin, Lin Xiang, Lu Chao, Wei Huai, and other staff members from various ministries and commissions, totaling about 500 people, attended. After Chairman Lin led the ceremony, President Wang was originally scheduled to attend the report. Later, President Wang temporarily changed to Chairman Lin to report "Political Work Over the Past Year" due to attending the Executive Yuan's routine meeting, saying that today is the last day of 1934, which is also the last memorial week of this year. Now, the general report on political work over the past year is as follows: (1) Military Bandit Suppression: Military affairs depend on Chairman Chiang's proper deployment and the soldiers' obedience to orders. The bandits in Jiangxi have been completely suppressed. The remnant bandits who fled to Hunan, Guizhou, and Sichuan have been definitively planned, and a staff group has been formed to enter Sichuan to supervise the suppression. The remnant bandits can be suppressed in a short period of time. In addition, the public security in North China depends on Minister He's seat in the town and Chairman Huang's proper handling. Military officers and local authorities have also maintained their strength. Achievements have been made in receiving refugees, resettling wounded soldiers, and stabilizing local order. Military training in various places has made particularly significant progress in the past year. (2) Foreign Affairs: Our country's foreign policy is based on the Prime Minister's legacy of peace and struggle. On the surface, it seems that there has not been much progress in foreign affairs over the past year, but our country's peaceful attitude and credibility in diplomacy are well-received by all countries except those with ambitions. (3) Finance: After various provinces and cities abolished exorbitant taxes, the central government, in consideration of the inadequacy of local finance, allocated stamp tax funds to the localities to compensate. Regarding the silver issue, a few speculators previously smuggled silver exports. Since the Ministry of Finance stipulated anti-smuggling measures, the outflow of silver has ceased, and Minister Kong and the Shanghai banking community have explained it. The current financial situation has been stabilized. (4) Education: In recent years, the government has actively promoted production education, which has gradually become effective. In the past year, students sent to study abroad have focused on practical science to cultivate national production and construction talents. (5) Transportation: With the cooperation of the military and civilians, the construction of national highways has developed rapidly. The Longhai Railway has been opened to Xi'an, and the Huai River diversion project is in active progress. Important projects are expected to be completed in the short term. This is a general overview of the administration over the past year. Finally, he also stated that the construction of Beijing has made great progress. The development of education has made rapid progress, especially the eradication of opium, gambling, and prostitution, and the implementation of the New Life Movement have been quite effective. He also hoped that we will strive for reform in the coming year and improve the country's position. (Central News Agency Dispatch from the 31st)

Retrospect of Eastern Provinces in the Past Year

Farmers and Businessmen Bankrupt Under Japanese Iron Heels

Volunteer Army Continues to Rise Up and Resist Japan

Changchun Correspondent of the Chinese Alliance News Agency: Looking back at the Chinese people in the four northeastern provinces in 1934, they are still sinking under the Japanese slave policy. In March of this year, the puppet Pu Yi was proclaimed Emperor. September 18th was the 3rd anniversary of the September 18th Incident. On December 1st, the Japanese and puppets changed the four provinces into ten provinces without authorization (and divided East Mongolia into four provinces: East, West, South, and North), depriving the puppet provincial governors of their powers. The new administrative regions resembled Japanese prefectural governments. Recently, Japan has reformed the organizations in Manchuria and changed the security of the leased territory of Kwantung Prefecture and the railway affiliated areas to be managed by the military police, making all four eastern provinces under the iron heels of the Japanese military and political system. Rural bankruptcy is becoming more and more serious, and countless Chinese businessmen in the Northeast have gone bankrupt. Only the volunteer armies in the eastern part of Jilin and Liaoning provinces and the Heilongjiang province, numbering more than 100,000, continue their anti-Japanese work. Their patriotic sincerity and the spirit of not being seduced by fame and fortune have truly made the Japanese army tremble. In short, the people of the Northeast eagerly hope to regain their freedom as soon as possible, and their feelings are intense.

Japanese Obtain Free Commercial Lease Rights in Northeast

Immigrants Can Fully Operate in the Future

The Policy of Annexation is One Step Closer

(Tokyo) Regarding the "Manchukuo" case of Japanese commercial leased land, there have always been concerns about misunderstandings in various aspects, so the authorities prohibited recording it. This time, all negotiations on this issue have come to an end, and the ban has been lifted. The contents of the negotiations are as follows:

(1) In the past, under the Zhang Zuolin regime, only Japanese were allowed to have commercial lease rights to land within Liaoning Province. Now, "Manchukuo" automatically recognizes commercial lease rights in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces.

(2) At the time of the establishment of "Manchukuo," there were concerns that large capitalists from mainland Japan would advance to it. It was heard that only 150,000 cho of commercial lease were allowed, and the limit could not be exceeded. However, this restriction will not be added this time, and Japanese are allowed to freely rent it.

(3) The above-mentioned Japanese "Manchu" commercial lease rights negotiations have been completely and satisfactorily resolved. From now on, the term of commercial land leased by Japanese in "Manchukuo" is 30 years (the term can still be renewed after the term expires).

Immigrants and other free points can be fully active in the future, so the close economic connection between Japan and Manchukuo in the future can be expected to develop. (Japan United Electric from the 31st)

A Japanese Military Train Derails at Suizhong Station

(Tianjin) A Japanese military train that departed from Shanhaiguan on the 29th, carrying 108 members of the Kwantung Army, three heavy artillery pieces, and a large amount of military supplies, derailed when traveling to Suizhong Station because the switchman mistakenly moved the switch. Twelve people died and 34 were injured. The artillery and military supplies were severely damaged, and the train was completely destroyed. When the train derailed, the artillery shells exploded, destroying the railway tracks. Two passersby were injured by the explosion, and three railway staff members were injured. The switchman has escaped. The Japanese transported the dead and injured to the Jinzhou Hospital, saying that the incident had a background and was making every effort to search for the perpetrator. (Special Dispatch from the 31st)

(Tianjin) A Japanese military train that departed from Yuguan eastward on the morning of the 29th derailed completely at Suizhong Station because the switchman moved the switch incorrectly. Twelve Japanese soldiers died and 34 were injured. Because the train was carrying ammunition, the vibration was too great, and the entire train was blown up. In addition, two pedestrians and three railway staff members were injured. The switchman fled immediately after causing the accident. (Central News Agency Dispatch from the 31st)
