Shanghai Girls' Middle School Fourth Anniversary Special Issue of Morality and Art

Foreword

— Lin Kanghou

The vast Pacific Ocean, the fierce waves are rushing, what time is it today. Sharks compete for the continent—what is the continent? It is the Chinese nation. Therefore, insightful people work hard on education—in the principles of education, there are actually many items listed: first Ke loves what he loves, and Zi likes what he likes. ...

My Chinese nation, with a population of 400 million, and among the 400 million, women account for half. Unfortunately, after the three seasons, they have become accustomed to customs and habits, spending their entire lives in seclusion, rarely seeing the faces of living people. Alas, women's bodies are willing to be played by men. Between the importance of men and women, a clear distinction is made from now on!

The ancestors had a warning: "Lack of talent is virtue." Ban Zhao wrote "Lessons for Women," and Duke Zhou wrote "Internal Rules." Women's models and rituals are discussed in detail, entering only to manage the dustpan and broom, and going out must be elaborately dressed; ... Song Confucianists were too busy, concerned about losing their chastity. From then on, women's bodies no longer had the light of day!

When Qing was coming to an end, all doors were opened, and the fruits of Western equality came to China. By the time we entered the Republic of China, what a majestic atmosphere. In major cities, girls' schools are densely arranged. Although we cannot catch up head-on, we are eager to catch up straight away. Girls' schools at this time are shining in five colors.

My school has been established for only four years. After several years of difficult management, we have finally achieved a satisfactory result. However, it is difficult to succeed, and it is almost certain to know the difficulty. The upper and lower levels must be of one mind, and the inside and outside must be one body. If we can be diligent, if we can abide by the principles, if we do not succeed, pluck out my eyes.

All female students, the most important thing is cultivation: in ordinary times, you must be quiet and idle, and be careful of drifting away in times of trouble. Studying should be diligent. Put an end to the thought of seeking luck, do not hold a hoof and wish for a full harvest; clothing should be simple, and take what is suitable for concealing the ugly. Do not apply powder and rouge, and act like a spoiled model.

My school is in its infancy, and the period is like a transition. In the past, we faced Wen Chao Street, but now we have moved to Xieqiao Road. In the past, when it was established, there were only a hundred students, and now it is considerable, increasing by ten or five times. We are grateful to the people of society for their praise. To plan for permanent ease, we will think about building from now on. From now on, we will think about what kind of building to build. In the quiet place of South Shanghai, purchase more than a hundred acres of land. In the future, we will close it as a school, and strive for large-scale. The square must be vast, and the houses must be spacious. There are rooms for experiments, and there are libraries for books... Although we cannot do it now, we will show our plans in the future. I am ashamed to be in the ranks, and this is difficult to shirk. I will write a few lines of ink for now to express my sincere heart.

Shanghai Girls' Middle School Fourth Anniversary of Cultivating Virtue and Art

— Inscribed by Lin Sen

Talking About Girl-Centered Education

— Ou Yuanhuai

Shanghai Girls' Middle School is scheduled to hold a school anniversary celebration on New Year's Day of the 24th year of the Republic of China, and a letter was sent to me, borrowing it to encourage the celebration. The reason is that the school has only been established for four years, and those in charge of school affairs have worked hard and managed it with difficulty. Today, it has become a very successful educational institution in Shanghai. I would like to take this opportunity to share my humble opinion with the people of the country on the issue of female education.

In the past, the general society in our country had an unreasonable view of women. The so-called lack of talent in women is virtue, the so-called three obediences and four virtues, this kind of patriarchal thinking has bound Chinese women for thousands of years. Therefore, the movement for gender equality is an inevitable trend in our country to adapt to the times. However, if we want to achieve gender equality, we must first raise the knowledge of women, and women's education will flourish.

However, our country has advocated the establishment of women's education for thirty or forty years. In the process of this new movement, on the one hand, there has been a lot of progress, and at the same time, many mistakes have been discovered. Girls' schools at all levels often only stick to the principle of gender equality in education, and are ignorant of the differences in male and female physiology and needs. They only focus on cultivating social people, and ignore the cultivation of family people. As a result, the disadvantages have caused many new-style women to only know how to consume, disdain to work, and cannot serve the society when they enter, and cannot manage family affairs when they retreat. The impact on the collapse of family organization and the crisis of the country and society may be more than we can say.

In the society of the 20th century, gender equality is generally recognized by the world, and equal educational opportunities are also stipulated by the constitution. However, so-called gender equality does not mean that whatever men do, women must also do. As for equal educational opportunities for men and women, it refers to equal opportunities for education in law, but in the content of educational facilities, there should still be different adaptations to characteristics. In other words, women should have women's education, which is also called girl-centered education. This new trend in education must be able to develop women's own femininity and women's common motherhood. The common humanity of mankind, in the family, must be a virtuous hostess, in the society, must be a productive member, and in the country, must be a sound citizen.

Based on the above, the facilities of girls' schools in the future, whether in terms of curriculum, teaching materials, equipment, or training, should not be completely given "masculinized" education, and special consideration should be given to the various situations of women's physiology, psychology, and society. Must focus on family economics, infant care, child education, hygiene principles and practices, and sex education guidance, etc., in order to maintain their natural talents, spiritual qualities, and special interests and emotions, and be able to cultivate a new era of independent and self-conscious women, who can serve the society externally and maintain the family internally, which we are happy to see. And the future of the country really depends on it.

For the Shanghai Girls' Middle School in the Past Four Years, Cultivate Virtue and Study

— Inscribed by Jiang Zhongzheng

The Past of Our School

— Wu Zhiqian

Education is the foundation of a country. The prosperity and decline of a nation and the strength and weakness of a country depend on the transfer of its culture. The countries of Europe and the United States, with their advanced academics and pioneering science, look down on the universe and are rich and powerful. Observers attribute this to the popularity of education. Our country has been weak for a long time, and the national power is declining. Revitalizing and strengthening depends on the development of education and the construction of the national economy. The transformation of the country depends on the transfer of the people's wisdom. My country has a population of 400 million, and women account for half of it. Therefore, the education problem and the career problem of women must be solved. This is the reason why I founded Shanghai Girls' Middle School.

In the spring of the 20th year of the Republic of China, I gathered comrades and raised funds. Then, I rented No. 19 Xuexi Street, Wenmiao Road, Ximen as a school building, and hired Mr. Lin Kanghou, Chu Minyi, Wu Tiecheng, Wu Xingya, and Tao Baichuan as school managers. I published an advertisement in the newspaper on January 22 to recruit students, held the first entrance examination on February 9, and officially started classes on the 14th. From then on, our school officially met with the public.

In the autumn of the 20th year, the number of students increased sharply, and the original school building was not enough for use. Therefore, I rented Jialu, Menghua Street as an off-campus dormitory and completely transformed the original school building into classrooms. As for the subjects, it is divided into four departments: high school, junior high school, kindergarten normal school, and adult remedial class. I thought that the foundation of the school was already in place, and from then on, it would be able to proceed smoothly, not remembering that not long after the start of classes, the disaster of "September 18" occurred. The bad news came, and the whole country was angry. The teachers and students of our school embraced the motto of "reading and not forgetting to save the country, saving the country and not forgetting to study," and rose up to organize an anti-Japanese association to advocate for all schools; they also organized a propaganda team to go to places such as Su and Xi to publicize, awaken the people, and jointly go to the national crisis. Looking back on this semester, the minds of all the teachers and students of the school were occupied by the work of resisting Japan and saving the country.

In the 21st year, our school was about to endure the pain of starting classes, but the "January 28" Songhu Incident occurred again. Therefore, the students were scattered, and the impact on our school was indeed great. In the autumn of that year, due to the impact of the war, the high school department was temporarily suspended; a simple normal department and a Chinese-English typing department were added to meet social needs.

After the start of the spring semester of the 22nd year, school affairs developed, and the original school building was too narrow. Therefore, two large houses on Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road were rented as school buildings, which is also the current school building of our school. In the autumn of that year, the high school department was restored, divided into ordinary vocational departments; and the Hunan Guild Hall was rented as a sports field. Since this year, the foundation of the school has become more and more consolidated. Now, in total, there are high school, junior high school, vocational department, normal department, typing department, remedial department, and affiliated elementary schools and kindergartens such as Dalu, Daguang, Zhenhua, and Tianhua. There are more than 800 students and more than 50 faculty members.

Although our school has only been founded for four years, the foundation of the school has been laid. Tracing back to the source, although it can be said to be the efforts of our school colleagues, it is also due to the support and assistance of people from the society. In the future, we will continue to work hard in accordance with our original intention. We hope that the people of the country will rise up and teach us!

Shanghai Girls' Middle School's Progress in Virtue and Scholarship over the Past Four Years

— Wang Zhaoming

The Current Situation of Our School

— Lu Zhongkui

It has been four years since the establishment of our school. Through hardships and difficulties, and with painstaking management, the teachers and students of the whole school have worked together to develop the school affairs to the scale of today. The actual situation has been described in detail by Principal Wu Zhiqian as above. Since I have been serving as the teaching director of our school, and I have been doing my best for two years, on the occasion of the fourth anniversary of our school, I would like to briefly describe the current situation in points, and report it to the people of the society. I hope that you will point out any omissions:

1. Organization Our school takes the board of directors as the establishment body. The school administration is fully managed by the principal, and the secretary assists the principal in handling school affairs. School affairs are divided into two departments: general affairs and teaching, each with several sections to handle daily school affairs. In addition, various committees are set up to manage the affairs related to each committee.

2. Meetings Our school handles school affairs on the principle of rationalization. In order to gather wisdom and benefit from each other, the handling of various school affairs must be submitted to the meeting for public decision. The school affairs meeting is the highest administrative meeting of our school, and it is organized by the directors of various departments and affiliated institutions and representatives of faculty members, with the principal as the chairman. It is held once every two weeks, with general affairs and teaching meetings set up below, with the directors of each department as the chairman, and held once every four weeks. There is also a general meeting of all faculty members, held separately at the beginning and end of each semester. The life guidance committee is organized by the class teachers of each grade, and it is held once every four weeks.

3. Rules and Regulations In order to achieve division of labor and cooperation, and to have each position have its own responsibilities, our school has certain rules and regulations for administrative processing and student activities. The more important ones include organizational outlines, faculty service regulations, temporary faculty treatment regulations, school affairs, general affairs, teaching, and various student rules, etc.

4. School Buildings The current school buildings of our school are all rented. There are two large buildings in the middle school department, covering an area of six mu. There are more than one hundred and twenty rooms of various sizes.

5. Equipment Due to limited economy, the equipment of our school is simple. There are now offices, reception rooms, auditoriums, ordinary classrooms, special classrooms, libraries, physics and chemistry instrument rooms, conference rooms, entertainment rooms, student dormitories, dining halls, and faculty dormitories, which are sufficient for application. In addition to ancient books and the first and second collections of the newly revised Wan You Wen Ku, there are more than 5,000 books. There are more than 1,000 pieces of physics and chemistry instruments, specimens, and hanging pictures, worth more than 2,000 yuan.

6. Faculty In this semester, there are a total of 23 faculty members in the middle school department of our school. Two-thirds of them are excellent, and more than three-quarters of them are full-time. Two-thirds of the graduates of universities and specialized schools are also strong, and the appointment is based on specialized subjects. Female teachers account for more than one-third of the total.

7. Students In this semester, there are more than 800 students in the junior high school spring and autumn grades, the high school ordinary vocational departments, the simple normal department (which is being closed), the typing department, the remedial department, and the affiliated elementary school.

8. Curriculum The curriculum of our school is in accordance with the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, and it is modified according to the actual situation, with Chinese, English, and mathematics as the main subjects, and special emphasis is added.

9. Teaching Materials The teaching materials for each subject in this semester are all based on the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry, and the latest and best teaching books on the market are selected, or they are compiled by the teachers in charge of each subject.

10. Teaching Our school's teaching adopts strict doctrine. Academic and moral behavior achievements are practically examined on time. Entry and exit, correspondence, meetings, telephone calls, and requests for resignations are all managed. Dormitories are checked early and late, absences are strictly handled, student group activities are guided, school life is enriched, educational movies are opened, field trips are held, academic research is encouraged, and the New Life Movement is promoted, in order to achieve the balanced development of morality, intelligence, physique, and beauty.

3 Daguang Elementary School and Kindergarten

4 Dalu Elementary School and Kindergarten

The Future of Our School

— Zheng Tiejian

Our school was established four years ago. We have been planning painstakingly and managing diligently. Today, it has taken initial shape. Looking back, with extremely limited financial resources and a short period of time, the fact that we have achieved today's results is primarily due to Mr. Wu's efforts. Observing the current situation, the school's development is now a thousand times greater than in the past. However, we colleagues are unwilling to be complacent and will continue to uphold our original aspirations and strive forward. This is what we sincerely want to tell the ladies and gentlemen of society. On the occasion of our fourth anniversary, I would like to elaborate on the school's future plans as follows:

I. Material Construction

Material construction requires sufficient financial resources. Once the economy is sufficient, large school buildings, spacious campuses, sports fields, classrooms, libraries, and science laboratories can be completed in succession. In order to realize the Shanghai Girls' High School in its plan, our school specifically purchased land in Caohejing this summer for the construction of a new school building. At the same time, we established a school development committee to raise huge funds and implement a five-year plan. All future facilities of our school will be based on this plan and will be carried out diligently to achieve a good educational environment.

II. Non-Material Construction

An excellent school must develop equally in quality and quantity. Quantity is only the form of the school, while quality is the spirit of the school. The future facilities of our school must seek a balance between the two. The so-called non-material construction includes the following:

(1) Teachers: Hire teachers with noble character and outstanding academic ability to teach various courses and instruct students.

(2) Curriculum: In addition to focusing on the three basic subjects of Chinese, English, and mathematics, we will also strive to enrich and perfect other subjects such as natural sciences, social sciences, hygiene, and arts.

(3) Student Training:

(1) Healthy Physique: Establish sports fields, promote healthy entertainment, pay attention to daily life and diet, exercise their bodies, and cultivate hardworking, resilient, energetic, and physically and mentally strong citizens.

(2) Enterprising Spirit: Change students' decadent and negative outlook on life to a positive, courageous, and enterprising spirit. Not only must they have the integrity not to do evil, but they must also have the intelligence to do good, so that they can shoulder the heavy responsibility of transforming society.

(3) Scientific Ability: Cultivate a scientific mind, treat people and handle affairs with a scientific attitude, be organized, increase work efficiency, and encourage students to study science and make scientific explorations and inventions.

The above are the fundamental guidelines for the future facilities of our school. We know that this work is arduous and difficult, but "where there is a will, there is a way." Our colleagues will work hard with an indomitable spirit to achieve it.

Shanghai Girls' High School has excellent management and teaching, promoting Chinese culture and emphasizing practical learning, cultivating talents and exuding fragrance, the teaching staff has its own source, and the virtue of women is greatly demonstrated. Four years of operation have resulted in a complete scale, and collective wisdom and efforts are making progress day by day.

— Sun Ke, inscribed for the fourth anniversary of Shanghai Girls' High School, New Year's Day, 24th year of the Republic of China

Free Talk

New Year's Day

— Xiang Yu

The "edge of the clothes" of the past year still remains in our eyes.

We sighed a long sigh of relief. Good or bad, we have spent another year. Disappointment is falling behind, and hope is running ahead. Readers, if well-intentioned blessings are not rejected because we are in the same state of sorrow, let us, on the first day of this new year, temporarily cut off the sorrowful time we experienced in the past year and the unpleasant events associated with it, and let us open our arms to welcome this new year and its associated hopeful future. Of course, we cannot erase the facts and close our eyes and say that our suffering has gone with the past year, and our bright future has come with the coming year. People who say such things vaguely are either deliberately deceiving people or are following the old example of saying auspicious words such as "Congratulations and get rich" to make the listener happy. The fact is that no matter how auspicious words are said, how many are said, or how pleasant they are, they are not of much use to reality. (People who like to hear auspicious words have a different psychology and should be treated separately.) The objective situation will never change because a few auspicious words are said. We know that in such an economic downturn, we don't know how many people are on the hunger line, we don't know how many people are on the death line, we don't know how many people are throwing themselves into the Huangpu River, we don't know how many people are unemployed, we don't know how many shops are preparing to shrink, and we don't know how many shops are preparing to close. Even if auspicious words are willing to be said, who will listen? Undoubtedly, auspicious words, although not superfluous, are meaningless. Therefore, the so-called "happy new year" is actually unhappy.

Therefore, the arrival of the new year is like a stranger, an unwelcome guest, an unfortunate fate for most people, who do not want it to come, but have to let it come. Everyone has to step forward and experience it. The course of time cannot be exceeded or stayed, but the personnel in the evolution associated with time are somewhat controlled by ourselves. The imperfection of personnel is not the fault of others, but our own lack of effort. The center of the problem lies here. Should we face the problem head-on and work hard to untie the knot of the problem? Or should we retreat to the side of the cemetery and sing a decadent song? A lone boat in a rushing current on a stormy night can only move forward and not retreat. If it moves forward, the harbor may be in front of it. If it retreats, there is nowhere to stand and wait. In the course of life, there is only survival and death, and there is absolutely no bargaining. So it is with organisms, and so it is with superorganisms—society—toward survival—forward; toward death—backward. This is the New Year's example, and it is also the words we encourage each other with.

New Year

— Zang Kejia

Some time ago, I passed by a small alley, and a pair of door couplets evoked freshness in my eyes. As time passed, I no longer kept this in mind. As the New Year approaches, my heart is touched, and the pair of door couplets floats before my eyes again.

"The new year is not new,

The old year is not old."

You will find it ridiculous when you see it, right? However, after laughing, can you find some meaning in it?

Since China adopted the Gregorian calendar, there have been two years standing opposite each other. The new year gives the new people in the city excitement, while the old year still gives the old people in the countryside freshness.

If you say that the new year is indeed new, I cannot refute it, because every time we celebrate the new year, the atmosphere in the city is indeed different from usual. Every household hangs the flag of the blue sky and white sun, government officials hold New Year gatherings, and schools and shops can also be freed for three days. The happiness of a series of gongs and drums and a few tables of banquets come together. The authorities announce new plans, and various professional groups also set a new plan, as if after the new year, everything is really renewed and changed into a new life.

However, in other aspects, poor people in the countryside after bankruptcy are really afraid to say that they are celebrating the new year. When the new year comes, not to mention starving in the depths of spring, in their hearts it seems that every year is worse than the last. This is not superstition at work, but the lessons of reality.

The person who created the phrase "The new year is not new" must have the same feeling as me, right?

New Year's Nonsense

— Wei Zhongtian

My life has really become too bad this year. I myself sometimes can't believe why it has become so bad. Since I don't understand, if there is really such a thing as "fate" in the world, then I have to ask "fate" to understand.

When I celebrated the New Year last year, I was in ×× place. It wasn't happy or sad. I ate chicken and braised pork, and on that day I also saw a friend spit out a lot of bright red blood! This friend was spitting blood because of unemployment. A healthy person can also spit blood. This gave me a very deep impression. Not long after, I spent an old New Year in Guangzhou. At this time, because I had just escaped from the disaster, I felt a little happy—I only lived in Guangzhou for a week, and the great wind of life blew me to a city in the west again. I lived in pain and boredom for a few months. Although I only lived there for a few short months, that city gave me a lot of memories. These memories are naturally all painful! It was also at this time that I was shot in the heart by an enemy's arrow, and I almost wanted to leave this world for a short time. Even now, this scar still hurts.

Finally, in August, I decided to leave that painful city and flowed to Shanghai with a broken heart. I haven't seen Shanghai for a year, and I think it's a little thinner. I thought to myself: Shanghai, what extent will you be thin in ten years?

I only lived in Shanghai for more than a month, and I left it again. This time I left Shanghai was very accidental, and I left Shanghai with hope and a new heart. From this time on, I rebuilt my self-confidence and felt that I was still young. If I could work hard, the future would not be hopeless!

And now it's New Year again. The days are as fast as shooting arrows and as fast as lightning. Another year has passed quietly. What have I gained this year? Nothing at all. What I have is still the same disappointment.

This year's New Year is spent in Tokyo. This is the first time to spend the New Year in a foreign country. Of course, I have to wear a smile. Where will I spend the New Year next year? If there is really such a thing as "fate" in the world, then I have to ask "fate" to understand.

People Who Don't Know New Year's Day

— TK

Year-End Musashino

— Xiangshan

In the year-end in a foreign country, one is infected with a country sickenss, that is so vague, light and lingering, like the evil pole on a black festival night, listening to the clear and slight bell sound of the church, so lingering and light.

The sky is becoming clearer, in the early morning, pushing open the shoji window, the sky on the tangerine branches seems solid, throwing stones at the sky, making a worrying sound, this sound wave does not spread like spring waves, but like a cluster of arrows shooting at the sky; ah, it is deep winter, this solidified sky ah: far away in a remote alley, the desolate sound of the tofu vendor's trumpet, like the howling of the Huns outside the Great Wall, will bring you a desolate feeling.

Even though there is no longing for the homeland, the power that can lead you to indulge in longing is deeply hidden in the secret heart. All beauty and art are often imprisoned in the shackles of fantasy. When reading Gide's "Pastoral Symphony," one can envy the life of the blind! Fantasy and recollection, like lyrical poems, decorate the dilapidated with beauty and splendor.

Like a lark tired of singing, resting in the desolate Musashino in a foreign country, it is the end of the year, Musashino has dried up small rivers, withered grass, and broken old wooden bridges. This lark, faintly, caresses all the scenery with its eyeliner, skimming over the hills, and resting on the tombstone in the cemetery behind a desolate Bodhi temple. There is a blood-red red bead tree in front of the tomb.

I am like this lark, the desolate Bodhi temple at the bottom of Musashino has often become my strolling place. Musashino contains touching love stories. The flavor of history and the elegies of many poets, but for me, an exile, Musashino only has simplicity, which fascinates me, especially when listening to the wind in the wilderness of Musashino at night and reading Kunikida Doppo's Musashino Diary. This kind of interest is a synthesis of simplicity and fantasy.

When the sky is clear, on the prairie of Musashino and the tops of the withered trees, Mount Fuji, with its snow-covered top, stands out conspicuously. The charm of Fuji is completely concentrated in the snow on the top, which is white and does not melt; that kind of cold feeling, like a sharp sword, pierces into the body and mind, and one tastes satisfaction in a kind of shuddering.

Musashino not only gives a simple feeling, but also reminds people of many natural waka and haiku. These "songs" and "verses" give the most obvious contrast to Mount Fuji and Musashino. The wildness is like a spring. When your eyes look down at a piece of soil and a blade of grass, you can feel it deeply.

"The mountains are vast and the night has covered the sky, but only the peak of Mount Fuji still lurks in the twilight." This is Tayama Katai's song about the scenery after dusk in Musashino in winter; the vast sky of Musashino is covered with a slightly black and thin pattern, and the peak of Mount Fuji is particularly contrasted with its snow-white color, so it feels like a test of the memory that is still in the twilight. This kind of vague emotion is like gazing at the posture of a geisha with a Shimada-style headdress in the Yoshiwara red-light district under the willow trees on a foggy street, which is full of imagination.

Although there are only distant mountains and the Tama River and small streams, without a rare flower or a magnificent house, the toilet bowl placed next to the rice field, the toilet bowl with black crows perched on it, seems to have a kind of simple beauty and the smell of a farmer's house.

Especially during the day, the field is scattered with red and green flowers, which are the children in the village who are collecting field vegetables and alfalfa; they are wearing red and green tattered clothes, and with surprised eyes and exploring expressions, they are digging out their own food. This kind of energy and seriousness in life makes a wandering foreigner feel the alienation of life.

It is already winter, it is already the end of the year, those villagers carrying bamboo and pine on their backs are rushing to the city to decorate the Kadomatsu of the city people's homes (Japanese people all insert pine and bamboo in front of their doors during the New Year), and the cut-off roots of pine and bamboo that have been chopped off by the road one by one all have folded white marks, dotted in the withered grass.

Just waiting for the snow to fall, at that time Musashino will be wearing plain clothes, Mount Fuji will be wearing a plain crown, a kind of sad feeling will give anyone a heart that wants to shed tears, but they don't know the unspeakable emotion of where the tears come from.

Although Musashino has history, love, and a part of time and space, my love for Musashino is only for its simplicity, and the "haiku" and "waka" that I recall along with Musashino.

Winter Musashino is not decadent and desolate, it is more simple and can comfort people who are exiled in a foreign country near the end of the year.

Home Night Vignette

HAPPY NEW YEAR!

A Son with a Wife (Part 1)

— Yu Qijin

Old Fu Yun walked over limping. His body was so thin, hunched over; walking so weakly, panting and coughing. When he came closer, he put on a forced bitter smile on his gray face, and said tremblingly: "Sir, I beg you to write a letter for me."

I responded repeatedly, oh, oh, and dragged a bench for him to sit on.

"The letter is to my son, cough, asking him to put his ass down a little more steadily," a look of resentment appeared on his lips, "Speaking of my son, I can't breathe."

"Speak slowly, say whatever you want, I'll write it for you." I couldn't find words of comfort.

"That's right, sir, I'll have to take up a lot of your time, my words are very long! Don't hate me, I have to tell you the reason why I want to write this letter first." He seemed a little pleading.

"No, I have nothing to do, you can talk slowly."

"Alas, I always envy others. Not to mention anything else, like sir, your father is really lucky! To give birth to such a good son, ……" "What nonsense, what's so good about it!" I interrupted him, "Please tell me the reason why you want to write a letter."

"Er, er, yes, sir, I'll tell you. I remember very well: Thirty years ago, when my son was born, how excited my wife was! She would say dozens of times a day: "Ah Jun's dad, we have someone to rely on when we get old!" But, alas, my wife died before me; who knows, instead of relying on my son when I'm old, I'm suffering from my son!

His eyes were a little wet, and I could only say yes, but there was no way to comfort him.

"Five years ago, I married a wife for my son. Everyone in the village said: Old Fu Yun is really lucky. But who knows! After my daughter-in-law entered the door, my cheekbones became so high. When my clothes were tattered, -- just like now, -- people asked me with surprised expressions: Old Fu Yun, your clothes are not good, ask your daughter-in-law to mend them? I shook my head, and at this time I felt that they understood that I was not lucky, but was suffering!

"A son without a wife is still okay. He works in Shanghai, and at the end of the month, he sends a letter to my father, and sometimes attaches some copper coins for me. But in these five years, I have not received a letter from my son, -- what else to say about copper coins. -- Even if my son comes home, I want to talk to my son about my suffering as a friend, no, I can't, this daughter-in-law will stand opposite my son and stare, this stare seems to be saying: You don't have to soften your heart, you don't have to pity this old thing.

Flies (Part 4)

— By Pirandello, translated by Xi Dichen

They had been beating for a day and a half, and only a few almonds had fallen. The female workers proposed that they peel them all that night, peel them until late at night, and then just sleep there randomly, so that they could get up and return to the village early the next morning. They really did that. Lopa took the cooked beans and two long glass bottles of wine. The peeling work was completed in the middle of the night, and all the male and female workers lay down on the threshing floor and slept quietly. The grass left on the threshing floor was wet, and the dew was like the sky had really rained.

"Sing, Leola"!

Nelly sang immediately. The moon passed in and out of the thick net of small black and white clouds, and the moon was like Thursa's round face, which sometimes smiled slightly and sometimes frowned as the joy and sorrow of love rose and fell.

Chai Lu was once kept in the stable overnight. Salo ran to wake him up before dawn, but saw him swollen all over, black all over, and having a fever with boiling heat.

The above is a piece of what Nelly told the barber clerk. The barber clerk only listened, and inadvertently, his attention shifted to a point, and he cut him with his razor. Near his chin, he cut a small, small wound, which was nothing to speak of. Nelly didn't have time to think about it again, because at the entrance of the barbershop, he met Rusa and her mother, and also met Nita, Shimia, the poor girl promised to Chai Lu, who was crying sadly.

After all kinds of persuasion, this poor little man understood that she could not go to Montrusa to see her lover; they tried their best to call him back, and she would see him before dark. Salo also rushed over at this time, saying loudly that the doctor had already gotten on the mule and was not happy to wait any longer. Nelly dragged Rusa away and asked her to be patient; before dark, he would come back and have many wonderful things to say to her.

For lovers, really, even other people's emergencies are some wonderful words; when you talk about it, you hold hands and look at each other.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Ode to the New Year

— Chen Liang

When I was a child, I often had a dream: "It would be great if we could celebrate the New Year every day." Even adults, as long as the rice jar at home is fortunately not empty, who wouldn't want to happily celebrate a few days?

The New Year is filled with peace, happiness, and hope.

For example, when you sleep in bed in the morning, even if you are awakened by Ah Da and Ah Er fighting for rice cake dumplings or throwing firecrackers, you are not getting enough sleep. If it were a normal day, you would inevitably scold "little devils" a few times, but during the New Year, this anger will never rise, and maybe it will become very affectionate, and you will give the little mouth a few sweet kisses, or even make a few impromptu promises, such as buying toys, making new clothes, or taking them to see a play. As for whether it will be implemented or not, it is up to you, and the children will always smile at you to show their goodwill, even when they find out that they have been tricked, the New Year has already passed anyway.

Also, for example, if you have been suffering from financial troubles and embarrassment for the past few days, you can completely forget about it during the New Year. Two friends who almost caused a police incident on New Year's Eve still greet each other with smiling faces and congratulate each other with hands cupped, "Get rich, get rich," their hearts filled with an extraordinary joy. Also, some people inevitably show some poverty at the end of the year, but when you meet him during the New Year, you have to listen carefully to his report on the wins and losses of gambling, and he seems to be very rich again.

Furthermore, for example, when eating at home, small disputes may inevitably arise on weekdays, such as complaining that the salted yellow croaker is too light because of your poor appetite, blaming the hard rice because of toothache, or complaining about the children's bad eating habits. But these things will never be taken to heart during the New Year. During the New Year, we must try our best to avoid the occurrence of all disputes. Even if something unexpected happens, and the children blurt out a few unlucky words, it must also be included in the "no taboos" column.

Moreover, the New Year is also a time for repentance, determination, and making vows. People who suddenly wake up from a daytime dream will say: "The past is like yesterday's death, and the future is like today's birth." The New Year is the beginning of the year, putting aside all the past behaviors of prostitution, gambling, corruption, and perversion, and then arranging a procedure on the spot on how to turn over a new leaf and how to work hard, or even friends who have never written before actually bought a three-sided diary, preparing to put out perseverance to write hundreds of words a day. During the New Year,

You can make more great wishes and generate more hope. As for what will happen after the New Year? There is no need to consider it during the New Year at all.

In short, all the phenomena of the New Year are fresh, vigorous, and energetic. The New Year is a day worth praising and celebrating!

The Prelude to 1935

— Cheng Quan

The cold wind blew ceaselessly throughout the night.

Dawn arrived, and a touch of gray light permeated the sky, hazy like a winter dusk. A vagrant huddled in the street corner, yawning, and opened his eyes: day had broken.

Rubbing his sleepy eyes, he stood up and peered out onto the street. The street was deathly silent. After a whole night of being trampled by passersby, it seemed injured, gasping for breath, yet also sinking into a deep slumber. Grayish-white frost covered the road, like the pallid face of a sick person.

Shops, one after another, were shuttered with iron gates. The national flags, hung out the previous night, flapped and danced incessantly in the cold wind. A sign stood straight at the entrance: "Happy New Year—Closed for three days."

Suddenly, a jolt: Another year had begun.

Looking at the sky: The sky remained deathly still.

Could it be that another year had slipped away? Yes, it couldn't be wrong, could it? Looking at the red-lettered newspaper in the hands of the deliveryman, looking at the red "January 1st" in the calendar vendor's hands, a thousand wrinkles seemed to form in one's heart: There was no mistaking it, another year had indeed passed.

Thinking: In this era, even individual wandering has become a global phenomenon. When the whole world has fallen into a season of wind and rain, perhaps everyone feels a bit unwell? We've already been battered by wind and rain for quite a few years; but why do those sufferings never seem to end? The world is like a train entering a mountain tunnel, endlessly dark.

(A streamlined 1935 Citroen sedan, packed with drunken people, men and women, wearing paper hats from a masquerade ball and releasing colorful balloons, rushed by aimlessly.)

In this era, being able to put oneself into a state of numbness might be happiness.

The cold wind hadn't stopped, and as it blew, one shivered: Everyone hopes the sun will rise sooner, everyone hopes for a warm spring.

Like a prayer, like a New Year's blessing, silently praying, one looked up at the sun. The sun was still hiding in the dark clouds, and one's heart sank, and one smiled unconsciously.

(Children were throwing firecrackers in the street, their sounds drifting clearly across the street. The sky was gradually brightening, and various people were walking on the street: office workers on holiday, students on break.)

A new atmosphere.

Yes. When a new year arrives, everyone gives themselves a new hope, a new beginning, right? Whether it is beautiful or ugly, people step into this year, and they must instinctively live on.

Each year is like a book. When we open the first page of a new book and begin to read its first word, who can know what it will contain?

But whether it is good or bad, it is always a new beginning.

It is said that 1936 will be a tense year, so 1935, which is right next to it, may not be an ordinary one. In the face of this coming year, there are two things: survival and death, joy and misery.

An era that progresses to this stage of tension is worth celebrating. Surely there are some more glorious events ahead: the glory of survival!

But whether it is light or darkness; whether it is an endless storm or a day of sunshine; come, come quickly!

Let us pray for this new 1935! In this season of wind and rain, let us hope it is a glorious one!

Another Year

— Wu Ye

Time passes like scenes in a movie, flashing before one's eyes. The 365 days of a year slip away in an instant. Ah! Truly, "time flies like a river"! I sigh as I remove the old

Page 39

calendar from my desk and replace the vacancy with a brand new calendar for the 24th year of the Republic of China.

A year has passed, and another year strides into the world. Naturally, in this quiet coming and going, I have grown another year older, and my life's history must lightly turn another page. However, let us examine this past page: Is there anything sufficient to comfort the past and encourage the future? I dare say that in the past year, encouragement and comfort are out of the question. Apart from aging by one year, everything else remains the same!

What gifts, then, shall I prepare to celebrate the beginning of this new year? In this year, there is nothing to rejoice over, and even less need to offer praise or prayers. However, unadulterated pessimism and despair are also inappropriate. The matters that stand before us still require us to struggle and to work: whether it is political encouragement, educational construction, rural relief, social reform, commercial revitalization, national strength, or the respect of morality... all rely on the cooperation of the government and the people. Only by cooperating and working together can we achieve success.

Looking back at our country in the past, whether in politics, society, the nation, or the people, we have almost always been groping in the dark, struggling in the darkness. The nation's troubles at this time cannot be denied. Natural disasters and man-made calamities are rampant, and internal and external problems are severe. The suffering endured by our people is truly unbearable to recall.

We now hope to find comfort in struggling from suffering, and to strive for light in the darkness. Naturally, we have great expectations for the coming new year. As for whether these expectations will be realized, that remains to be seen in the future.

Celebrating the New Year

— Hu Tianyu

I don't happen to be named Wang, nor do I go by Little Er, but fate has decreed that I am the same as Wang Xiaoer—each year worse than the last.

There is a saying in my hometown: "This year we hope for a better next year, [but] every year we wear a tattered cotton-padded coat." This saying is quite humorous, but unfortunately not very accurate. In my experience, I am indeed always hoping, today I hope for a better tomorrow, this year I hope for a better next year, but it is not necessarily "every year we wear a tattered cotton-padded coat." Saying this doesn't mean that my hopes have been realized, that things have indeed improved, that I don't wear a tattered cotton-padded coat, but rather wear a new cotton-padded coat, or a Western suit and leather overcoat. In fact, not only do I not have a Western suit and leather overcoat or a new cotton-padded coat to wear, but sometimes I even feel lacking in a tattered cotton-padded coat. Yes, didn't I get through one winter wearing a tattered lined robe?

To paraphrase the tone of "Fisherman's Song": "The tattered cotton-padded coat left over from the year before last, carefully I'll rely on it to get through another winter."

Now the New Year has arrived, the warm spring is about to descend, and soon I should be able to take off this very undignified tattered cotton-padded coat; because although I am poor, I am very fond of dignity.

May Everyone Not Waste This Year

Year's End

— Xu Xizhen

(The glass windows of a Vienna flower shop display Nandina and Wintersweet, a duet of red and yellow.

"Winter Solstice and New Year's gifts at great discounts, crowded every day, come quickly!")

Jazz music in a masquerade ball, a costume ball, red balloons, green balloons. A swollen Santa Claus, with a little trumpet in his hand, "toots" and laughs.)

Laughing, the boss of Tianfa Store said to his wife, "Don't worry, what's the use of worrying? It's the end of the year, but there's still a month or so until the settlement period. We have to get through this New Year season, come what may."

The wife was a little unconvinced, still wrinkling her brow, looking as if she was about to cry. The "Ah Da" in the store was also a bit suspicious, worrying that the market this year would be even worse, that there would be more failures, and that currency would be even more "impossible to circulate."

But the boss himself didn't believe it. He had started out "apprenticing" as a grocer, for at least twenty years. He had never encountered a year-end without a market. "Three spring seasons rely on one winter," otherwise, what kind of business could one do? He laughed at others for being foolish and fearing the sky would fall, for having narrow vision and being inexperienced.

But in fact, the boss might really be a bit muddled. Usually, someone who started out as an apprentice and spent twenty years in the "foreign goods business" would not fail to see that the market was getting worse every year, and that several stores would close down around every holiday season, not to mention—just talking about this year's "foreign Winter Solstice," they put up the red and green lights as usual, and hung up the flags with big discounts as usual, but the business was really not as good as last year. The money earned from selling for a week barely covered the "shop rent," and the labor was wasted! The boss didn't plan to think too much about these situations—perhaps he didn't dare to think. He placed all his hopes on the period before and after the settlement period. He knew very well that there was still a "Lunar New Year" waiting for him there, and he had to use all his energy to deal with it, to struggle.

But he may have carefully considered it in several late nights; two difficulties lay before him: inside was that his own store needed a little nourishment, for example, to paint the storefront and add some signs for advertising, or, if things went well, perhaps he could get a radio. In addition, the most important thing was that the store had to add some goods; but all of this was a problem because his own store was almost just a skeleton. Without cash, nothing could be done. And there was another major external obstacle, namely the malicious competition of larger-scale businesses. They used the advantages of large scale to lower prices to levels that smaller peers could not reach, and at the same time used the appeal of large advertisements to try to absorb as much cash as possible, and these were all the murderers who strangled the throats of small and medium-sized merchants!

These two enormous imaginary enemies, like two heavy shadows, pressed heavily on the heart of the Tianfa Store boss, desperately refusing to let go. He felt that this suffocation was dangerous. "Maybe one day, I will fall in front of my enemies."

However, although these difficulties oppressed him day and night, he refused to reveal them on his face. He was not a major entrepreneur, and of course lacked "iron willpower," but he also had his plans and his policies. The only solution at present was to first think of a way to "resist" (Note: to shift, to transfer) a little merchandise from several familiar "businesses" and prepare all his energy to deal with the "Lunar New Year" before the settlement period.

But the next day he got up early and ran to the familiar businesses he usually dealt with, he understood that things were not as easy as he had expected. The answers he received from each family were almost the same: "It's really hard to say, we are all old customers, is it possible that we don't trust you? But the inside instructed that from the New Year to the settlement period, all transactions will only be done in cash, and there will be no dealings—it's really not a good time, I'm afraid that there will be some places where things won't turn around at the end of the year—you know this difficulty."

These words may be true, but the boss of Tianfa Store was immediately pushed into an ice cave. He felt a chill and stood up to return to his store. Several shop assistants were flipping through the daily newspaper on the table. Suddenly he caught sight of the announcement of "×× Company Liquidation" and, as if he had received an inspiration, he casually asked a shop assistant:

"Is it still possible to send an advertisement to the newspaper within the year?"

"It's definitely possible, today is only the 26th, the newspaper's deadline for advertising is the 28th—New Year's Day, we'll have red newspapers to read again, a big stack!"

Sino-Western (1040) January 3rd

City Government Holds a Victory Celebration Assembly Against Bandits via Broadcast

9:00 PM to 10:00 PM Guanyin Society Reappears

Wang Ersao, a virtuous woman from Guocun, Ganxi. Her husband died after the Northern Expedition. Ersao served her ailing mother-in-law above and cared for her orphaned children below. Relying on a few acres of ancestral land, she and her children wove and farmed, barely managing to make ends meet. Her cousin, Songquan, was of ill repute and had long desired to seize her chastity and property. He frequently borrowed money from her for gambling, and when his wishes were not granted, he would nag incessantly. Ersao's young daughter, Xiuzhen, was engaged to Liu Guoliang, a primary school teacher, with a promise of lifelong companionship. Songquan denounced this as a family disgrace and demanded money incessantly. Later, he flirted with Xiuzhen, attempting indecency. Guoliang arrived in time and denounced him as a beast, angrily driving him away. Songquan harbored a grudge and sought revenge. When the Red Army approached, Songquan was recommended by his comrades and appointed as a scout, responsible for identifying wealthy farmers and local bullies. Once Songquan gained power, he led the Red Army to arrest Guoliang and forced his widowed cousin to remarry a scoundrel, coercing Xiuzhen to submit to him, or else Guoliang would be put to death. Xiuzhen plotted to free Guoliang, enduring humiliation and reluctantly dealing with Songquan. At this critical moment, the anti-bandit army entered the village victoriously, eliminating the wicked and pacifying the good. Guoliang, with his meritorious internal assistance, was appointed to a military post. The Wang family, mother and daughter, were able to see the light of day again. Xiuzhen and Guoliang finally became husband and wife.

Shen Bao Supplement for the Port Film Special

New Year's Greetings

— Reporter

Happy New Year! - As esteemed readers turn the first page of the 1935 film special, these four characters seem particularly appropriate.

Because it is the New Year, everyone is in good spirits, having eaten their fill of good food and wine, and heading to the cinema to spend a happy day in laughter.

Because it is the New Year, everyone is getting rid of the old and welcoming the new, like the new clothes and hats they wear, filling their hearts with new hopes. For example, hoping to get married and have children this year, hoping to have the opportunity to be active in the political arena this year, hoping to win the fifty-million-dollar jackpot this year - no, hoping not to be unemployed this year.

Because it is the New Year, those who are concerned about the country and its people are naturally not so happy. For example, the national crisis is deepening, and another year has passed. The economic panic is intensifying, and the number of unemployed is increasing, which is bound to become more acute this year. The Nine-Power Treaty is being scrapped, and the opposite of disarmament is the vigorous expansion of armaments. The Second World War is imminent, and the people of our country will inevitably become cannon fodder on the Far Eastern battlefield. To mention these things on the first day of the New Year would inevitably spoil the mood, and even make those filled with hope feel half-hearted. But it is useless not to speak, and silence cannot turn misfortune into good fortune.

Because it is the New Year, the gentlemen of the film industry naturally have new plans. For example, producers hope that their employees will work especially hard this year, increasing production. Audiences suddenly become rich and watch movies day and night. There will be more super-special productions to break last year's box office records. On the other hand, directors, cinematographers, set designers, and other middle and upper-level employees, in addition to hoping to produce world-class masterpieces of their own, also hope to get a raise from one or two hundred yuan to four or five hundred yuan. Even if it is highly unlikely, it doesn't hurt to have bigger hopes. Actors hope to leap to stardom this year, and stars hope to be crowned emperors or queens, leading to unveilings, faces becoming trademarks, and extra income, lots and lots of it. As for the laborers on the set, in addition to hoping not to be electrocuted to death, they also hope not to be kicked out of the studio by the company without any reason, so as to avoid their wives and children crying.

Because it is the New Year, the film special naturally also has some basic hopes. For example, the film special does not talk about "revolution" or "progress" in the first place. In this year, it is already very remarkable to be able to say a few words that must be said and can be said. At the same time, the film special always maintains a fair position, without flattery, without conformity, without carelessness, with obligatory publicity, but never attempting to take subsidies or blindly promote. Therefore, it is hoped that people will not misinterpret or undermine it. And the esteemed readers who love this publication are constantly giving us criticism and correction, which the reporter sincerely welcomes on behalf of this publication. As for the improvement plan of this publication, of course, there is one, but there is no need to make a big fanfare or brag about it before implementing it.

That's all for now. Looking back at the above, it doesn't seem to make the readers smile happily, but rather makes them feel puzzled. This is certainly not appropriate in this great New Year. But it may be remedied here, anyway, it doesn't hurt to be too polite, so let's have another one:

Happy New Year!

Film Reviews

Review of "The Highway"

— Ling He

Realism in film is emphasized and demanded in China. The film that accurately portrays reality will become a great work. Furthermore, we demand that filmmakers scientifically observe reality, and then correctly analyze and experience it, and then boldly and bravely, without any embellishment, express it in film works. In other words, whoever reacts to reality most actively is the greatest writer of the era, and therefore his works are most likely to be supported by the vast audience.

Indeed, at this stage we still have to demand a new romanticism, but this romanticism starts from reality. That is to say, from a correct understanding of reality, and a scientific determination of its inevitable future, that is to say, seeing the inevitable creation of tomorrow in today. This ardent yearning for the future is regarded as romanticism, but this is by no means an unattainable fantasy, but rather has a historical determining significance. Therefore, we demand a new romanticism, while we oppose romantic fantasy.

After watching "The Highway," the above words seem to need to be emphasized. This is because the romantic component in "The Highway" far outweighs the weight of realism.

When exploring the inner workings of "The Highway," we may as well observe it in connection with the author's previous works. Mr. Sun Yu, who is called a poet, in "Little Toys," he loudly shouted for the entire people to resist Japan and save China, and save themselves. He placed the task of saving China on the entire people, so he had ardent hopes for national industrialists, and at the same time, the broad masses of people opposed imperialism, and the gentlemen and ladies standing on the balcony of the dance hall also opposed imperialism. From this point of view, it is naturally lacking in reality, but the author's passionate romanticism is fully expressed. Later, his "Sports Queen" put forward a brand-new view of sports, and at the end put forward the conclusion as romanticism, that is, the popularization of sports. Of course, this future outlook starts from reality, giving people great comfort. But now we see "The Highway," which is in the same posture as "Little Toys."

In "The Highway" and the prologue, the inspiration that the author gives us in his theme song (Pioneers of the Road) is "Thousands of years of fossils have accumulated into the mountain peaks on the ground. There is no road ahead, and human beings do not communicate. Who is hindering our progress?..." So he shouted: "Stand up with chest, unity don't loosen!" "Sighing is useless," "We are the pioneers of the road," "We will detonate the explosives buried underground and aim at them to blow!" "The earth is turned upside down, the mountain peaks are blown down, and the road is easy to start."... Here, his enthusiasm for the future of mankind is expressed in a majestic tone. So who will bear this great responsibility? The author places it on the broad masses of workers. In "The Highway Song," he wants the road workers to "carry the heavy burden and move forward!" "Everyone work hard, move forward together!" "Flatten the ruggedness on the road, crush the difficulties ahead," "Fight together," "No retreat, only forward." But this kind of enthusiasm is pinned on a non-realistic story, that is to say, "The Highway" is not a real expression. The most important thing is that he beautifies the lives of the road workers, and it is different from the fact that people in the play like Li Lili and Jin Yan are non-realistic characters.

Naturally, the author's consistent upward spirit and the expression of brightness, joy, and vigor all illustrate the greatness of the author's spirit. But it is in this situation that it proves that the author has neglected reality, no, perhaps he is deeply aware of the pain of reality and overcomes this pain with the glory of the spirit. It is very clear that when the road workers are tortured by traitors, he fully expresses the spirit of calmly facing death in the characters in the play. But that kind of cellar, Li Lili's flirtation, that kind of alertness and bravery, all make people wonder; is there really such a thing in the world? In this way, "The Highway" is inevitably very weak in terms of reacting to reality. As for the military officers and local bullies standing in opposition, and even helping the road workers, etc., it is also very worthy of discussion. And the point of "the spirit is immortal," although it is a true expression, is impeccable in terms of intention.

However, we always feel a great interest in this work. That bright tone, that firm spirit, and the excellent use of the sound effects of the dubbing, all express the content of the work in every aspect.

In all respects, this "The Highway" is not much different from "Little Toys." Everything that Mr. Sun Yu had in "Little Toys" reappears in "The Highway." Indeed, the author is a poet, a passionate poet. He hates ugliness, and he yearns for the bright future, but he does not face the essence of ugliness squarely, and at the same time, he does not pursue the bright future in a down-to-earth manner. However, we have ardent expectations for him, hoping that in the near future, he will change from the romantic style that does not start from reality.

Various other technical aspects are omitted due to space limitations.

Film Novel

A Nurse's Romance (The White Parade) (Part 2)

— Su Yin

After Long Nawaier and Nao fell in love, he persuaded Nao to stop her nursing work and marry him to be his wife. But Nao did not agree and continued her studies. At this time, Qi Jie, because she knew a training doctor in the hospital named Moore, often went out to play with him after work in the afternoon and returned to the hospital late at night. The nursing supervisor in the hospital warned Na for returning late many times, violating hospital rules, and told her that she should prepare a sum of money to go home for a comfortable holiday.

That was Nao's last year of internship in the hospital. One day, Nao attended Long Na's birthday celebration. Because of the hospital's rules, she had to return to the hospital early. But Long Na did not allow her to go back, and Nao insisted that he send her back earlier. Therefore, a quarrel occurred between them. Later, Long Na could not resist her and sent her back to the hospital early. However, at that time, Long Na had drunk a lot of wine. On the way home after sending Nao to the hospital, the car had an accident, and Long Na was seriously injured and was taken to Miche Lee Hospital for treatment. After a series of surgical treatments, he gradually recovered his strength, but after staying in the hospital for several weeks, he asked the hospital to send Nao to be his exclusive nurse. Nao refused because she had already promised another female patient not to leave her when she was in pain. Because Nao refused to break her promise to that patient, she had to let Long Na be angry. Nao's behavior was deeply admired by the general public in the hospital, especially by the chief of surgery, Dr. Tony, who said that Nao was the most reliable person. At the same time, Dr. Tangmin's wife had a disagreement with him and specially ran to Paris to file a divorce lawsuit. Tangmin felt extremely painful in his heart at this time. Fortunately, Nao understood his heart and comforted him from time to time. Tangmin's feelings for Nao deepened.

At this time, there was only one week left before graduation. Qi Jie was expelled from school and could not graduate because she had returned to the hospital very late for three consecutive nights, so the joint council of teachers and staff unanimously decided to expel her. Qi Jie was extremely sad. What made her most sad was that Dr. Moore, who often took her out with him, was indifferent. That day, Long Na happened to have recovered well in the hospital and was about to leave the hospital. Nao specially asked a classmate to replace her work so that she could send Long Na off. When she was about to leave, she suddenly remembered that she had forgotten to hand over the key to the anesthetic medicine cabinet to her replacement. In a hurry, she handed the key to a servant who opened the elevator, and the servant handed the key to Qi Da, because Qi Da was going to the room where the anesthetic medicine cabinet was placed. Unexpectedly, Qi Jie took the key, secretly opened the medicine cabinet, and took a lot of morphine to swallow in an attempt to commit suicide. Fortunately, she was discovered not long after taking the poison. So everyone hurriedly rescued her, and Qi Da was thus able to celebrate her birth. However, because of a momentary negligence, Nao almost caused a major incident. According to the hospital's rules, she should be dismissed. However, Tang Ni tried his best to intercede for her, so Nao was able to retain her position.

That strange southern girl, Enna, did not study her work carefully, and she was indifferent to the exam. But when the graduation exam results were announced, she passed safely. Not only did she graduate and pass, but she also pitied Qi Da and planned for her, and even restored her original position. All of a sudden, a class of students was struck by a bolt from the blue, wondering what kind of magic power Enna had. Later, they learned that her father was the financial agent of this hospital, so she had the right to freely dispose of the hospital's administration. They had their graduation ceremony. After the graduation ceremony, Long Na came again to ask Nao to give up her nursing career and marry him to be a rich young mistress. But Nao felt that she should serve the people, so she sacrificed the vanity of a social leader and took up a nursing position. As a result, she got Dr. Tony's entire understanding, silently expressed his approval and admiration to her, and a romance ended here. (End)

Shen Bao Architectural Weekly

Summary of the Shanghai Municipal Library and Museum Projects

— Dong Da You

Constructed by Zhang Yutai Construction Company

I. Introduction

Culture is inseparable from life. Urban areas are where populations concentrate, making cultural development particularly urgent. Shanghai's residents have already reached over 3.4 million. Yet, existing cultural facilities are either too small or simply lacking, a truly regrettable situation! Recognizing this, the Shanghai Municipal Government designated a vast area in the city's center for an administrative district, allocating a portion for cultural facilities and encouraging private groups to lease land there to establish venues related to cultural education and exhibitions. In early 1934, the municipal government and most of its subordinate bureaus moved into the central city area, laying the groundwork for the Greater Shanghai Plan. Considering the urgency of cultural development, in addition to planning a municipal sports field southwest of the administrative district to meet citizens' needs for physical exercise, they also proposed building a municipal library and museum within the administrative district to provide citizens with resources for learning, research, and observation. The municipal sports field has already broken ground, and its outline has been reported in a separate publication. Now that the foundation stone of both the library and museum has been laid, a brief description of their architectural layout is presented below for the information of people from all walks of life.

II. Library

This library is located in the administrative district of the city center, between Fuqian Right Road and Funan Right Road, south of Fuxi Outer Road, facing east: opposite the museum. The floor plan is shaped like the Chinese character "工" (gōng), with the front part extended horizontally at both ends, projecting forward and backward to form wing-like structures. The maximum distance between the north and south ends is approximately 66 meters, the maximum distance between the east and west ends is approximately 51 meters, the building area is approximately 1,620 square meters, the total area of each floor is approximately 3,470 square meters, and the volume is approximately 25,000 cubic meters.

The majority of this library is a two-story building, with an average external wall height of approximately 12 meters. However, a gate tower is located in the center of the front facade, with its roof ridge approximately 25 meters above the ground (see the front and side views of the library). If there is a need for expansion in the future, there is no need to increase the height of the existing building; simply adding buildings of the same number of floors in the remaining space behind it can more than double the capacity.

The exterior of the library building adopts a hybrid style of modern and Chinese architecture, as purely Chinese styles are too expensive and not entirely practical. The gate tower is covered with yellow glazed tiles and adorned with ornate eaves, with a stone railing surrounding its platform, fully displaying Chinese architectural characteristics. The entire building is a reinforced concrete fireproof structure, with the external walls constructed of artificial stone. A large platform is set up in front of the main entrance, planted with flowers and trees. Flagpoles are erected on both sides of the platform to enhance the view.

Regarding the layout of the ground floor interior, the central entrance leads to a large hall, approximately 12 meters wide and 13 meters deep, connecting to the corridors on both wings and the grand staircase to the upper floors. Behind the hall is the magazine and newspaper reading room, approximately 17 meters wide and 14 meters deep. Further back is the book storage, approximately 30 meters wide and 11 meters deep, leading directly to the back door. This book storage is a particularly tall single-story structure (external wall approximately 13.5 meters high), to accommodate five-tiered steel bookshelves over two meters high. The total length of the arranged books is approximately 15,000 meters, with a capacity of approximately 400,000 volumes. The lower floor of the left wing houses various offices, and the lower floor of the right wing houses the children's library, rare book storage, and lecture hall (approximately 10 meters wide and 18 meters long).

The central part of the second floor is divided into two sections, with an exhibition room in the front, approximately 22 meters wide and 13.5 meters long, and a lending library and catalog room in the back, approximately 17 meters wide and the same length as the front. The left and right wings are corridors, study rooms, and special reading rooms, with reading rooms at the horizontally extended parts at both ends, approximately 26 meters wide and 10 meters long, each accommodating 150 seats.

Above the central front part of the second floor is a mezzanine, used as a storage room, from which one can reach the flat roof behind and ascend the gate tower via outdoor steps. This gate tower can be used as an exhibition hall, and its surrounding platform can be used for sightseeing. A portion of the area beneath the magazine and newspaper reading room is excavated to build a basement for boiler installation.

The interior of the hall, lending library, and exhibition hall are decorated in a purely Chinese style with magnificent decorations and vermilion columns. The floors of the staircases and corridors are paved with polished stone, the floors of the reading rooms are paved with cork blocks, and the floors of the remaining areas are covered with inlaid sandalwood and rubber blocks.

The library's construction budget is estimated at 300,000 yuan, excluding the construction cost of the steel bookshelves inside the book storage. Zhang Yutai won the bid for the construction project, which commenced in September 1934 and is expected to be completed in August 1935.

III. Museum

This museum is located in the administrative district of the city center, between Fuqian Left Road and Funan Left Road, south of Fudong Outer Road, facing west, opposite the library. The floor plan shape is similar to that of the library, but the two ends of the front wing only protrude forward (see the museum floor plan). The maximum distance between the north and south ends is approximately 60 meters, the maximum distance between the east and west ends is approximately 58 meters, the building area is approximately 1,900 square meters, the total area of each floor is approximately 3,430 square meters, and the volume is approximately 19,000 cubic meters.

The central part and the two front wings of this museum are two-story buildings with an external wall height of 10.5 meters. A gate tower is added, with a roof ridge approximately 24 meters high. The protruding parts of the two front wings and the two rear wings are single-story buildings with a wall height of approximately 6.5 meters (see the front and side views of the museum). The future expansion plan of this museum also aims to add buildings in the remaining space, and the building area after expansion can be doubled.

The exterior appearance of the museum is generally the same as that of the library, but the beams and columns of the gate tower are exposed, and fountains are set up in front of the protruding parts of the left and right wings to enhance the decoration. The entire building is also a reinforced concrete fireproof structure, and the external walls are built with artificial stone.

In terms of the interior layout, the central entrance on the ground floor is the hall, approximately 17.5 meters wide and 14 meters long, with stairs to the upper floors and cloakrooms and sales rooms attached. From here, the door leads to a large hall, approximately 11.5 meters wide and 18 meters long, where the main staircase is located. On both sides of the hall are corridors leading to offices, study rooms, and storage rooms in the left and right wings of the front part. The protruding part of the left wing is the library, approximately 10 meters wide and 15 meters long, with a capacity of approximately 100 seats. The protruding part of the right wing is the lecture hall, with the same length and width as the library, with a capacity of approximately 300 seats.

The second floor is arranged with three sections in the center as exhibition halls and sculpture halls. The one in the front is the largest, approximately 17 meters wide and 14 meters long. The two wings are calligraphy and painting exhibition halls, each approximately 11.5 meters wide and 25 meters long, covered with glass skylights.

Above the central two-story front exhibition hall is a mezzanine, with the ground level flush with the flat roof in the back. From here, you can reach the gate tower on the fourth floor via outdoor steps. A platform is also set up around the gate tower for sightseeing. There is a basement under the hall for setting up boilers, etc.

The interior decoration aims to create an appropriate background for the exhibits. The hall and main exhibition hall are decorated with red columns and palace-style painted railings and flat ceilings. Most of the floors are paved with polished stone, the floors of the important exhibition halls are paved with inlaid sandalwood, and the corridors are also paved with polished stone. The lighting in each exhibition hall aims to project most of the light onto the exhibits without causing reflections into the eyes of the audience. The area where paintings are hung receives light from the upper side, so that it shines obliquely on the wall, allowing the audience to face the bright paintings in the shadows, making them clearer. The lighting equipment adopts an "indirect" style, the purpose of which is the same as above. Because the exhibition halls on the upper floors do not have windows and rely on glass skylights for lighting, artificial methods must be used to replace the air. The building has a built-in ventilation system that distributes cold and warm air according to the season.

The construction cost of this museum is estimated at 300,000 yuan, and Zhang Yutai won the bid for the construction project. Construction commenced in September 1934 and is scheduled for completion in August 1935.

IV. Conclusion

The above description only covers the engineering aspects of the library and museum in the central area of Shanghai. As for the equipment aspects, such as the collection of books and magazines and the search for exhibits, efforts should be made to achieve completeness to meet the needs of promoting culture. However, this matter is of great importance and cannot be accomplished overnight. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will assist from the sidelines and jointly contribute to its success. This is sincerely wished and prayed for!

Model of the Shanghai Municipal Library

— (Constructed by Zhang Yutai)

Model of the Shanghai Municipal Museum
